Mexico Considering Withdrawing from the League of Nations 50

Mexico City, Mexico: Mexico previously announced its withdrawal from the League of Nations due to financial difficulties (this was in 1932), and then immediately declared its re-entry. It is now about to announce its withdrawal again. According to the latest news reports, based on the opinions of the members of both the Senate and the House of Representatives, this move could be decided on Wednesday. "The League of Nations is a costly and ineffective organization, and its demise is not far off. After Paraguay implemented its withdrawal in February of last year, other Latin American countries will inevitably follow suit. This organization failed to provide any assistance in handling the disputes between China and Japan and the Chaco War. Recently, it has been at a loss for what to do about the dispute between France and Germany. What it does is no different from a puppet, and it cannot continue to deceive people for long. Its absurdity and darkness have been seen through by the world." (Havas dispatch on the 20th)

British and French Representatives Consult; Cracks Appear in the League of Nations Structure; Executive Council Passes Resolution with Benevolence and Righteousness; Makes Final Peaceful Appeal to Italy; Abyssinia Expresses Regret Over Accommodating the Aggressor 51

(Geneva) The results of today's Executive Council meeting have created an unfavorable impression, as the debate did not reveal genuine unity among the member states. The speeches of British Foreign Secretary Eden and French Cabinet member Pang Gu allow one to see the differences in their opinions. Observers believe that the cracks in the structure of the League of Nations are almost visible at a glance. Before the resolution was passed, all members of the Executive Council made speeches, and it was heard that several countries, including South American countries, opposed placing the blame for undermining reconciliation on any one party. (Reuters dispatch on the 20th)

(Geneva) The Executive Council of the League of Nations continued its non-public meeting at 6:40 PM today and then held a public meeting at 10:10 PM, at which it unanimously passed a resolution to record the failure of the mediation of the Italy-Abyssinia dispute, stating:

Full Text of the Resolution

"The Executive Council hereby takes note of the report submitted by the Committee of Thirteen. The Committee previously applied on March 3 for Italy and Abyssinia to swiftly cease hostilities and restore peace within the framework of the League of Nations and in accordance with the spirit of the Covenant of the League of Nations, and the Executive Council hereby ratifies this. It should also be noted that the Abyssinian government accepted the commencement of peace talks on March 5 in order to resolve the dispute. It is regrettable that the reconciliation work ultimately failed, and the war not only failed to stop but continued, which is in conflict with the Covenant of the League of Nations and has been declared as such. Therefore, the various obligations stipulated by the Covenant must be implemented. In view of this, the Executive Council hereby makes a final appeal to the Italian government. As a founding member of the League of Nations, and in the current situation where cooperation between countries is most urgent, the country should demonstrate a spirit to resolve the dispute and live up to the expectations of the League of Nations. Furthermore, all countries signed a protocol on June 17, 1925, mutually prohibiting the use of poisonous gas, and there are also other international protocols signed successively regarding methods of warfare. Both Italy and Abyssinia are signatories to these documents and are bound by them. All countries that participate in these documents should abide by them, which is what the Executive Council values."

When the resolution was put to a vote, only Italy voted against it, but since the country is a party to the dispute, its vote was not counted. After the resolution was passed, the representative of Ecuador, Chaldermik, stood up and spoke, stating a reservation that the country had already canceled sanctions against Italy, so the phrase in the resolution, "Therefore, the various obligations stipulated by the Covenant must be implemented," could not be accepted by the country. Subsequently, the Abyssinian representative, Walter, spoke, stating that Italy was waging a war of aggression and that its methods of warfare violated international law, but the Executive Council's resolution did not mention this, which was regrettable. Furthermore, the Covenant of the League of Nations contains clear provisions for member states to provide assistance to countries that have been invaded, but the Executive Council has failed to maintain its commitment to these provisions, which sets a bad precedent with endless consequences. After the speech, the Chairman, the Australian representative Bruce, announced the adjournment of the meeting, which was at 10:20 PM, only ten minutes after the public meeting began. (Havas dispatch on the 20th)

Speeches by Representatives of Various Countries; Eden Expresses Determination to Uphold the League of Nations; France Acknowledges That European Peace Requires Italian Cooperation 52

(Geneva) The Executive Council of the League of Nations held a public meeting at 3:00 PM today.

British Foreign Secretary Eden spoke first, stating the responsibility of each member state regarding collective security. His words were straightforward and received close attention from the audience. Eden stated that seven months ago, the League of Nations had decided that Italy's commencement of war violated the Covenant of the League of Nations. The governments of all countries must express their obligations during these critical times and clearly announce the policies they intend to adopt. The United Kingdom is prepared to further implement economic and financial sanctions. The use of poisonous gas in war has long been deemed illegal by Italy, Abyssinia, and eleven other countries, and is related to the residents of major cities around the world. It now appears to have been used to harm people who are completely unprepared for this type of poisonous gas. How can we stand idly by and remain silent? Can we be confident that our own people will not suffer the pain of being burned, blinded, or killed in the future? In general, the future effectiveness of the League of Nations for all the countries attending the Executive Council that may need the protection of the Covenant of the League of Nations will largely depend on the final outcome of the current issue. The United Kingdom is prepared to act in accordance with the policies of the League of Nations, and its progress will be the same as other countries, but no greater than other countries. If the League of Nations is fundamentally shaken and its future effectiveness is uncertain, then we can only consider the policies that we are responsible for adopting. Eden finally appealed to the member states to do their best to jointly uphold the authority of the League of Nations. (Reuters dispatch on the 20th)

French Minister Without Portfolio Pang Gu spoke next, saying, "We must now address the threat in Europe, so we must restore peace in Africa. To complete the construction of Europe, we must have the full cooperation of Italy. The situation of Italy should also be resolved. The Italian representative Aloisi said this morning that Italy has never intended to deviate from the Covenant of the League of Nations. This statement is gratifying." Pang Gu further explained that the situation in Europe has become complicated due to the violation of current treaties by a certain country and that ways should be found to remedy this.

Soviet representative Bodankin, who is also the Ambassador to France, spoke after Pang Gu, saying that the reason why the reconciliation efforts of the Committee of Thirteen ultimately failed was due to the League of Nations' weak attitude towards the aggressor. The more arrogant and stubborn the aggressor's attitude, the more lenient the treatment it received, which is regrettable.

Polish representative Komarnicki said that if the League of Nations makes another attempt to reconcile the Italy-Abyssinia dispute, Poland is ready to participate.

Argentine representative Granchi expressed hesitation about tightening sanctions against Italy and stated that regarding the Locarno Pact, he hoped that the signatories of the Locarno Treaty would maintain close contact.

Portuguese representative Vasconcelos, Danish representative Baudebierre, Romanian representative Antoniade, Turkish representative Suat, Chilean representative Ordini, and Ecuadorean representative Chaldernik spoke in succession, all expressing regret over the failure of the reconciliation efforts.

Spanish representative Madariaga (Chairman of the Committee of Thirteen) said that in his opinion, the implementation of Article 11 of the Covenant of the League of Nations should precede Article 16 (regarding sanctions), and that the general international situation is such that the responsibilities of the League of Nations will inevitably become more difficult. He hoped that Italy would show goodwill so that the reconciliation efforts might succeed. (Above, Havas dispatch)

At this point, the Chairman of the Executive Council, Australian representative Bruce, said that 52 countries have agreed to apply pressure within their capabilities to stop the aggression. This pressure must continue. If it is abandoned, then the entire principle of collective action and the regulations of human affairs will suffer a fatal blow. Member states must not take any action to undermine the collective action efforts represented by the League of Nations. Therefore, it is now necessary to re-examine the entire system of collective security in light of the events of the past seven months and seek the best way to improve the situation. As for the use of poisonous gas, it is an insidious and cruel form of warfare. (Reuters dispatch)

Italian representative Aloisi then stood up to respond to this issue, saying that all countries only know how to criticize Italy, but no one pays attention to the atrocities committed by the Abyssinian army that Italy has exposed. At this point, Abyssinian representative Walter declared that he would respond to what Aloisi had said. At this point, the Executive Council announced the adjournment of the meeting.

According to Article 11 of the Covenant, it is stated: It is hereby declared that any war or threat of war, whether it directly or indirectly involves any Member of the League, is a matter of concern to the entire League, and the League shall endeavor to prevent it in order to maintain peace among nations. At the request of any Member of the League, the Secretary-General shall immediately convene the Executive Council. It is also declared that any situation affecting international relations that is sufficient to disturb international peace or endanger the good understanding on which international peace depends, any Member of the League has the right, in the name of friendship, to bring to the attention of the Assembly or the Executive Council. (Havas dispatch on the 20th)

What we have done is like sailing; we have now weathered the waves and reached the shore. We bring with us the strength, justice, and civilization of Rome, and we can go anywhere and be successful." Northern Italian Army: Headquarters Moved to Taixi; Southern Advance Attacks the "Hindenburg Line"; Addis Ababa Covered in Placards Reassuring the People: Advising Against Believing Enemy Propaganda 56

(Rome) Italian East African High Commissioner and Commander-in-Chief of the Expeditionary Force, General Badoglio, recently issued a communiqué stating, "The Italian army in the south has advanced 100 kilometers from its front-line base in the Wogaidan Province, pursuing the Abyssinian army. The headquarters of the Italian army in the north has been moved to the city of Taixi." (Havas, 21st) Mogadishu: The fierce battle of Goianacobo ended on April 17th, resulting in the defeat of the Abyssinian army. In this battle, one Abyssinian soldier fired a machine gun at the Italian army, and was unfortunately killed. Thereupon, his wife took his place and fired the machine gun for six hours until she was captured by Filipino soldiers in the Italian army. She is truly a heroine. The purpose of this major battle was to clear the road to Daga Modyu, which is the right end of the fortified line between Daga Fort and Daga Modyu built by the famous Turkish general Vehip Pasha during the European War, the "Hindenburg Line." General Graziani's troops are now attacking the "Hindenburg Line" along the road from Gabirarda Ri to Sassabana. (Reuters, 21st) Addis Ababa: Political circles here deny reports that the Italian army has advanced to within a day's journey of Addis Ababa. The whole city is now plastered with notices reassuring the people, stating that the Abyssinian government has been in communication with all towns rumored to have been occupied by the enemy, including Suramita (100 miles from Addis Ababa on the road to Taixi), Ankober, Hua Hsu, Daga Fort, Xiga, and Harar. The Abyssinian people are urged not to believe enemy propaganda. At the same time, residents of the capital are still evacuating in droves, with only the military and police remaining in the city. The Abyssinian people are now withdrawing their savings from the Bank of Abyssinia, sewing them into canvas bags for concealment. (Reuters, 21st) Addis Ababa: Thousands of wealthy Abyssinian and foreigners, hearing that the Italian army is about to advance to Addis Ababa, have moved elsewhere today. Most shops have closed, and almost all doors are closed. Only the Abyssinian Queen remains in the city, serving calmly as usual. All embassies are full of their own nationals. Large tents have been built on the airfields and large stoves have been set up to provide three meals a day. Thousands of Indians, Arabs, and other British nationals are lying in the gardens of the British Embassy, which has gradually become the last center of activity in Addis Ababa. (Reuters, 21st)

British Armed Forces Budget: Totaling 790 Million Pounds; National Defense Expenditure Increases Sharply This Year; Chancellor of the Exchequer Explains to the House of Commons 57

(London) This year's budget, which is regarded as an armed forces budget, was submitted to the House of Commons today by Chancellor of the Exchequer Chamberlain. The galleries were unusually crowded, including many diplomats and representatives from overseas autonomous territories. There was, of course, a large turnout of Members of Parliament. At 3:33 p.m., Chamberlain presented his fifth budget amidst cheers.

The Chancellor first stated that one notable fact was that the surplus of the previous term was 3 million pounds, 2.5 million pounds more than he had budgeted. He had estimated an additional budget of 14 million pounds, but in reality, he raised 14 million pounds. This indicates an extraordinary willingness to contribute to national income. So far, the country has been able to cope with unexpected new financial demands with ease. This is something the country can congratulate itself on. The increase in national wealth and the expansion of commerce can also be seen from this. The operation of the Exchange Equalisation Fund is still profitable. In the past fiscal year, the national debt has been reduced by £4,500,000, and the amount of floating debt has also been reduced by £51,500,000. The amount of debt repayment has not been increased, and the figure for debt clearance remains at £124,000,000.

At the beginning of his speech, the Chancellor distributed a financial report stating that the total budget for the army, navy, and air force was £537,000,000, compared to £512,000,000 last year.

The Chancellor stated that he had decided to allocate an additional £110,000,000 this year for additional national defense expenditure outside of the announced budget. It is estimated that the new national defense expenditure for 1936-7 will be £10,000,000 for the air force, while the new expenditure required for the army and navy has not yet been determined, but may also require £10,000,000. The total expenditure for 1936-7, including supplements, will be £798,000,000. Although national expenditure will increase greatly, the Chancellor expects national income to increase as well. He estimates that customs and excise duties will amount to £314,000,000, an increase of £10,500,000 over last year. He also estimates that income tax revenue will be £248,000,000, an increase of £10,000,000 over last year. Increased business expansion tax revenue should increase. In addition to the expected increase in income tax revenue of £10,000,000, beer tax revenue may increase by £.000.000, tobacco tax by £3,000,000, and oil tax by £3,000,000, estimating inland revenue at £420,000,00. Based on current tax rates, the total income from all sources should be £776,000,000, and the shortfall will be £21,000,000. The government will revise the law in the future to prevent tax evasion, and will pay attention to those who live in the country but manage their assets transferred abroad, as well as so-called one-man companies. It is expected that this measure will increase income by 4 million pounds in one year. Attention should also be paid to so-called educational custody funds, as they are used to evade taxes. Assets given by parents to their children have always been tax-free, but the tax-free method is now being abolished, which will generate £2,500,000. He intends to make up the shortfall from this year's income.

Referring to the difficulty of military expenditure, the Chancellor said that it would not be fair if the entire cost of re-equipping the military were to be recovered from national donations over the next five years. If a disarmament agreement cannot be reached, national defense expenditure will soon reach its peak. In the future, part of this expenditure may rely on loans. The Chancellor announced that income tax will increase by three pence per pound and tea tax by two pence per pound. He also intends to withdraw £5,250,000 from the road reserve fund, so that the budget surplus can reach £500,000. The only benefit that taxpayers will receive is that the children's allowance will be increased from £50 to £60, and the married allowance will be increased from £170 to £180. In the budget, the plan to help disaster areas is to organize a company with a fixed capital of £1,000. 000 to provide financial assistance to small businesses. The Chancellor stated that the final estimate was revenue of £798,381,000 and expenditure of £797,897,000, resulting in a surplus of £484,000. The Chancellor's report on the financial budget lasted for one hour and twenty-seven minutes. He finished speaking and sat down at 5:00 p.m. (Reuters, 21st)

Europe's Serious Situation: Civilized Suicide Will Be Seen in Our Time: British Secretary of State for War Addresses Territorial Army Camp 58

(London) Secretary of State for War Cooper spoke to the Territorial Army in Munchster last night, saying that the situation in Europe today is more serious than in 1914. The stakes are higher, so the losses will be greater. The only real progress we have made since the European War has been the manufacture of more destructive weapons. This is nothing short of the suicide of civilization. The suicide of civilization may be seen in our time. Without the Territorial Army, I don't know how we would be able to defend Britain on a voluntary basis. Cooper also criticized the British church leaders for advocating that soldiers should fight for what they believe in as a wrong doctrine. (Reuters, 21st)

Japan Implements Continental Policy: Unifying Diplomacy and National Defense; Establishing a Three-Minister Conference of Foreign Affairs, Army, and Navy; Regular Meetings to Study Countermeasures 60

(Tokyo) In view of the tense international situation, the Japanese government has decided that, after the regular cabinet meeting every Friday, an informal three-minister conference of the Army, Navy, and Foreign Affairs will be held. (The Prime Minister will also participate when necessary.) The first meeting is scheduled to be held on the 24th of this month. The discussion will cover the general situation of national defense and diplomacy, and a free and candid discussion will be held from a broad perspective, agreeing on the fundamental policies that Japan should adopt. At the same time, opinions will be exchanged on the international situation in order to determine and adjust the general outline of concrete countermeasures for foreign relations under satisfactory coordination. The main agenda for the conference is roughly as follows: 1. Establishing the coordination and unification of diplomacy and national defense. 2. What practical methods should be adopted in accordance with the independent and proactive national policy of diplomacy? 3. What policies should be implemented to eliminate the Red Movement in East Asia? 4. Adjusting diplomatic relations between Japan, Manchuria, China, and the Soviet Union. 5. Fundamentally handling relations with Britain and the United States. (Domei News Agency, 21st)

(Tokyo) Japan's implementation of its continental policy is related to the fulfillment of the important mission of national defense by the army. The central military authorities, in response to the independent and proactive policy of the current cabinet, are devoting all their efforts to its realization. They are paying very close attention to the recent new situations in which the Soviet Union, Outer Mongolia, and China have unfolded. Comprehensively considering the current situation, observing future Sino-Japanese relations, it is recognized that there is no immediate way to adjust Sino-Japanese relations based on Japan's three principles for China, and to improve all Sino-Japanese relations. Therefore, the military authorities attach great importance to the current situation in the Far East. In order to implement the continental policy, it is necessary to first seek the fulfillment of national defense, so this point must require the serious attention of the people. Minister of the Army Terauchi said that the Prime Minister's speech in the Diet should reflect the general intention of the military, and will exchange opinions candidly with the cabinet members. After the Diet ends, Minister of the Army Terauchi's plan to fulfill national defense will gradually become concrete. Regarding budgetary relations, etc., officials are currently conducting concrete research. (Den Tsushin, 21st)

(Tokyo) The Kokumin Shimbun published an article today, stating that Prime Minister Hirota is now planning to clear all obstacles in the path of Japan's continental policy. Hirota has consulted with Minister of the Army Terada several times and reached a complete compromise. The military is now studying the following policies: 1. Closer cooperation between the Army, Navy, and Foreign Affairs Ministries. 2. Abandoning the "inertia" plan regarding the border dispute in "Manchukuo" and formulating a fundamental and permanent countermeasure policy. The military does not feel that the frequent changes in the Chinese government's policy toward Japan have caused Japan much suffering. Therefore, the military is now considering permanent policies, and the relationship between the Chinese government and the Kuomintang should be handled accordingly. The military believes that the intrusion of the Communist Party into Shanxi Province affects the administration of eastern Hebei and Chahar, and in turn harms the interests of "Manchukuo." Therefore, the Chinese government should be advised to quell the communist rebellion. (Reuters, 21st)

Japanese Government Considers Reforming Administrative Agencies; Baba to Be Appointed Vice Prime Minister 61

(Tokyo) The Japanese government is now considering a plan to reform national administrative agencies. Japanese Prime Minister Hirota recently said that he would cancel one or two administrative departments and merge them, and appoint several ministers without portfolio separately. Prime Minister Hirota and influential figures in the cabinet all believe that administrative reform must be implemented at the same time as the appointment of ministers without portfolio, so that the political system can be completely reformed. There are two methods for appointing ministers without portfolio, both of which are currently under consideration: 1. Appointing four or five people to assist the current ministers. Their responsibility is to plan important national policies. 2. Appointing a Vice Prime Minister. Prime Minister Hirota does not want to recruit figures from political parties as newly appointed cabinet members, so it seems that the second method will be adopted in the future. Finance Minister Baba, one of the important figures in the Hirota cabinet, seems likely to be appointed as Vice Prime Minister and Director of the Cabinet Investigation Bureau, an agency that investigates national policies. Minister of Commerce and Industry Ogawa is expected to succeed as Finance Minister. (Reuters, 20th)

Locarno Countries Ask Germany to Explain Four Points 68

(London) When the Locarno Treaty signatory countries held their second meeting in Geneva on the 10th of this month, the British and French representatives immediately agreed to base their demands on the French memorandum of April 8th, asking Germany to clarify the four points contained in its memorandum of March 31st. The four points are: 1. How can the mutual non-aggression pact proposed by Germany be integrated with the basic principles of the League of Nations, namely the principle of collective security? 2. What is the intention of separating the League of Nations Charter from the Treaty of Versailles and making it an independent chapter? 3. What is the content of the equal rights demanded by Germany on the colonial issue? 4. Regarding the current situation in Austria, the Free City of Danzig, and the Memel Autonomous Region, are there any immediate demands for changes to the current European borders? According to our reporter, British officials, unwilling to act hastily, will generally wait for the end of the French legislative elections, i.e., after May 3, before raising this issue with Germany. The wording will be as precise as possible, so that Germany can clearly explain its views on the European and colonial issues without any ambiguity. At that time, a memorandum will be attached, making various suggestions to reconcile the plans put forward by France and Germany, so that the mutual non-aggression pact proposed by Germany can be integrated with the French claims, one to implement the various principles of the League of Nations Charter, and the other to establish a mutual assistance system. Informed sources also said that Germany originally intended to demand that the signatory countries of the mutual non-aggression pact should remain neutral if Germany took action against non-signatory countries. The main goal of Britain is to dispel this demand. According to British opinion, the mutual non-aggression pact proposed by Germany, compared with the obligations stipulated by the League of Nations Covenant, should naturally take second place. (Havas, 21st)

US House Passes Bill to Expand Air Force Five-Year Plan; Naval Aircraft to Increase to 4,000; Senate Investigating Committee Releases Report Advocating Nationalization of the Arms Industry 69

(Washington) The House of Representatives today unanimously passed Rogers' five-year plan to increase naval aircraft to 4,000, which has now been sent to the Senate for consideration. The House also passed Max Hon's bill to establish aviation training classes in national universities, with methods similar to the current Army Reserve Officers' Training Corps. The House Military Committee believes that the vastness of the Atlantic and Pacific Oceans and the construction of aircraft carriers and improved aircraft effectiveness by major powers have made it impossible for us to avoid air force attacks. (National Telegram, 20th)

(Washington) The Senate Arms Committee today released a report, with the majority in favor, advocating the expansion of naval shipyards so that all US ships can be built entirely by the government. The report was signed by Democratic Senators Pope, Clark, and Bone, and contains the following recommendations: A substantial portion of the ammunition industry should be nationalized to adequately supply the army and navy with the ordnance and ammunition required from government factories during peacetime; The sale of US military inventions abroad should be prohibited. (Washington) Rear Admiral Sterneck, the Chief of Naval Operations, visited President Roosevelt today to request prompt approval for the construction of two new ships. Roosevelt's Speech; Determination to Strengthen National Defense While Not Forgetting the Good Neighbor Policy 70

(Washington) President Roosevelt delivered a speech to the annual meeting of the Daughters of the American Revolution today, stating that the government is determined to strengthen national defense while not forgetting the Good Neighbor Policy, and that there is no contradiction between the two goals. The current national defense strength is much stronger than before, and this is intentional. Aggressive war is definitely not the policy of the United States and is not included in the plans of the US Army and Navy. Our goal is to adapt to the needs of national defense, and we seek nothing else. The needs of national defense vary with changes in the international situation. If all countries can disarm, then the United States' need for national defense will also decrease accordingly. Unfortunately, the current world is not like that. However, our disarmament policy is clear: first, we propose to continue seeking international agreements to limit armaments. Even if this effort fails, we do not want to increase armaments, unless the expansion of armaments by other countries endangers our security, then we should consider other options. (National Telegram, 20th)

Sino-American Economic Talks to Continue for Two Weeks; Scope Wider Than Expected 71

(Washington) Treasury Secretary Morgenthau announced today that talks with the Chinese banking delegation led by Chen Guangfu may last for another two weeks. However, I do not believe this indicates an obstacle to the current talks, and he stated that the scope of the talks is wider than expected, so we intend to proceed deliberately. Regarding the rise in silver prices in the New York market, the Treasury Secretary stated that the silver prices held by the Treasury Department have not changed, so the reason for the rise must be that the business community believes that silver prices are higher than before. As for the rumors that the rise in silver prices is due to the Chinese currency being linked to the US dollar, Morgenthau declined to discuss it. Experts generally believe that this is the result of speculator activity, and that the markets in India and China are also more active. According to reports from here, India recently stopped purchasing silver and is now suddenly re-importing it, possibly due to increased imports. During the spring of this year, the volume of Indian imports exceeded seven times that of the same period last year, and nearly half of the highest record in 1930. At the same time, it is known that a small amount of silver is currently being shipped from London to China. Observers familiar with the situation believe that this is quite strange, but some also believe that individual merchants hope to sell it to the Chinese government, and the Chinese government will then sell it to the US to make a profit. Other observers believe that this silver is shipped to China and then transshipped to the United States. Currently, Sino-American talks are still strictly confidential, but there is a growing feeling here that the United States may agree to purchase Chinese silver to alleviate the pain that China claims to have suffered from the US silver purchase policy. As for the price issue, it is not believed here that the US price can be excessively higher than the world price, because the Treasury Department must also prevent political attacks at home. It is said that after the Sino-American talks are over, Chen Guangfu will go to New York to assist in establishing a New York branch of the Bank of China. (National Telegram, 20th)

A Certain Foreign Ronin Assaults European Police Officer in Shantou; Police Officer Seriously Injured; Two Ronin Arrested; Foreign Consulate Requests Jurisdiction from Municipal Government 85

Shantou Correspondence: The actions of foreign ronin in Chaozhou and Shantou have become increasingly arrogant recently. Smuggling and tax evasion have long become commonplace. Harassment of Europeans is also frequently seen. After a certain foreign cruiser arrived in Shantou a few days ago, the ronin, relying on its power, again engaged in an outrageous incident of assaulting a European police officer. It is said that a certain foreign ronin smuggling syndicate has been severely punished by the anti-smuggling authorities for smuggling rice, resulting in sluggish sales of smuggled goods. Recently, in addition to trying to expand sales in the interior, the ronin have also enticed traitors in Shantou, granting them the ostensible title of "Distribution Office of a Certain Foreign Firm" to facilitate the expansion of their business. They instructed them to set up shops and sell smuggled rice, exempting them from paying business taxes and not requiring them to obtain business licenses or pay any other donations or taxes. A general group of unemployed hooligans, blinded by profit, competed to obtain wooden signs from the syndicate bearing the name of a certain foreign firm for their business. In the past month, the establishment of such distribution stores has sprung up like bamboo shoots after rain. According to investigations, there are no less than a hundred stores in the city. Because rice prices have risen in recent months, the price of smuggled rice per bag is one yuan or several dimes cheaper than taxed rice. The psychology of the masses in the impoverished society is to be greedy for convenience, so those who flock to it are like ducks. Inspectors and anti-smuggling officers, in order to maintain government revenue, earnestly advised citizens not to purchase smuggled rice. If they repeatedly refused to listen, they would have to stop them. As a result, they were envied by the ronin, who regarded the police as enemies and always thought of harassing and insulting them. Around 3:00 p.m. on the 14th, police officer Ou Han of the Third Branch of the Public Security Bureau was on duty at the 15th section when five or six foreign ronin approached him and deliberately kicked him. Ou did not argue with them. Seeing that their plan did not succeed, the ronin walked along Tongping Road. At the intersection of Tongping Road, they deliberately stood in the middle of the road, obstructing traffic, and talked and laughed loudly. Police officer Zhu Rili of the section, believing that they violated police regulations, stepped forward to persuade them politely. The ronin did not listen and instead insulted Zhu, then even pushed Zhu to the ground and surrounded him, violently beating him. At that time, a special police officer for defense funding happened to be passing by and stepped forward to dissuade them, but the ronin ignored him. Later, a police team from the Third Branch came to relieve the shift and, seeing their colleague being beaten, were filled with righteous indignation and rushed forward to stop them. Only then did the ronin flee in panic, but two of them were captured by the police team and taken back to the branch for interrogation. It is said that one, surnamed Lin, and another, surnamed Huang, are citizens of a certain foreign country and work at a certain foreign firm at the end of Shanpai Street. They only admitted that a misunderstanding had occurred with the police due to language barriers and that they did not assault the police officer. The branch believed that Lin, Huang, and others assaulting the police officer was witnessed by many people, so how could it be allowed to be excused with sophistry? The injured police officer, Zhu Rili, was sent to the Gospel Hospital run by the British for an examination. After the hospital doctor examined Zhu, he found that Zhu had multiple injuries to his face and body, and he filled out an injury report. He sent Zhu back to the branch. At this point, Feng Gang, the head of the Third Branch, did not dare to act arbitrarily regarding how to handle Lin, Huang, and others assaulting the police officer. He telegraphed Song Dejian, the head of the Public Security Bureau, for instructions. Song instructed to transfer the case to the bureau for handling. After receiving the instruction, Feng handed Lin Yingjie and the others over to the Public Security Bureau along with the confession and injury report. The bureau, believing that foreign ronin did not abide by the police laws of their residence, and even assaulted the police, disregarded our government, and insulted our civil servants, felt that if this was not seriously negotiated, it would greatly hinder the police from performing their duties in the future. In addition to detaining Lin and Huang, the case was reported to the municipal government. After receiving the report, the municipal government, in addition to first contacting a certain foreign consulate by telephone, formally submitted a note to the foreign consulate on the afternoon of the 15th. It is heard that the foreign consulate has requested that the municipal government first send Lin and Huang back to the consulate for their own handling. (April 17)

Mid-Term Situation in the Suppression of Bandits; Brief Overview of Shanxi's Financial Situation; Military Expenditures Surge; Bandit Areas Spread, Revenues Sharply Decline 86

Taiyuan Correspondence: Shanxi's finances have long been in a state of exhaustion, due to the devastation caused by the provincial currency in 1919, and the vitality has not yet recovered. With the bankruptcy of rural areas and the stagnation of finance in recent years, both public and private finances have been very strained even before the Communist bandits disturbed Shanxi. The provincial treasury's income and expenditure were in deficit by more than 700,000 yuan per month. The arrears transferred throughout the last year were nearly 10 million yuan. While the authorities were trying to make up for it, the Communist bandits disturbed Shanxi, military affairs suddenly arose, and income sharply decreased. Its financial difficulties, from a global perspective, occupy the same important component as military affairs. Since the Communist bandits sneaked into Shanxi from northern Shaanxi, initially only occupying Zhongyang and Shilou, most of them were ravaged by bandit troops. Although the degree of damage varied, the scene of people supporting the old and young and fleeing in groups was the same. Up until recently, it has reached thirty or forty counties. In these areas, people have no time to pay public funds, let alone save their lives. Therefore, the province's income has completely come to a standstill. Moreover, Shanxi, a rich area in the province, is known as southern Shanxi. The province's tax revenue has always been rooted in the Hedong Road. This time, the bandit troops focused their attention on this area. The counties disturbed were mostly in southern Shanxi, so the sharp decline in the province's tax revenue can be imagined. As for the huge expenditures after the military mobilization, it is even more difficult to predict. In order to encourage morale, Yan issued a clear order from the day of the attack that each soldier would receive an additional four yuan and fifty cents per month on top of his original salary. Including other items, it is said that an additional 1 million yuan must be spent each month. If we add the previous deficit of 700,000 yuan per month, it would be useless to raise another 2 million yuan per month on top of the original income. The authorities are extremely anxious about this. In addition to repeatedly appealing to the central government for assistance, they have also repeatedly convened financial meetings to discuss ways to raise funds to make up for the deficit. Currently, in addition to the central government agreeing to provide monthly assistance of 500,000 yuan (some say 300,000 yuan), the province's fundraising methods have been either clearly ordered to be implemented or are being planned, including the following: In the entire province, except for the three counties of Zhongyang, Shilou, and Xi County, which were most severely affected by the bandit disaster, an additional tax of one yuan per tael will be levied. For all houses, if they are not self-occupied and are rented out, one-tenth of the rent income will be collected per month. Business stall taxes are determined differently depending on the situation in Taiyuan City. Donations will be deducted from the salaries of civil servants. Those who actually receive more than 600 yuan per month will have 70% deducted, those who receive more than 500 yuan will have 60% deducted, those who receive more than 400 yuan will have 50% deducted, those who receive more than 300 yuan will have 40% deducted, those who receive more than 200 yuan will have 30% deducted, and those who receive more than 100 yuan will have 20% deducted. Even those who receive as little as 20 yuan will have a deduction rate. Those who receive less can donate freely. All civil servants who receive public funds from the province or county will be subject to the above regulations and will be deducted by the disbursing agency. However, the deduction rate for the education sector is slightly lighter than for other sectors. The banquet donation is organized by the municipal government. It is stipulated that those with a菜价菜价 above 5 yuan will be charged one-tenth of the tax, and those with 菜价菜价 below 5 yuan will be exempt from the tax. The above measures have been clearly ordered to be implemented. In addition, there are anti-communist donations, but the amount is very small. It is currently planned to levy additional donations on luxury goods, etc., similar to the anti-bandit military vehicle period in Jiangxi Province. The implementation method is being researched, and it is heard that personnel have been sent to Jiangxi for on-site investigation, and it should be implemented soon. Among the above measures, the land tax surcharge and the deduction from civil servants' salaries are the largest amounts. However, with the spread of military affairs and the expansion of bandit areas, the original income has decreased invisibly. It is truly difficult to estimate whether the newly raised funds can replenish the loss of the bandit areas. Therefore, the authorities are still extremely worried about this financial problem. (Sent on April 18)

Bengbu Correspondence: More than a hundred bandits including Mao Xuehai and Zhang Jincai, who were wreaking havoc in Linyi, Shandong Province, were originally remnants of Liu Guitang's bandits. Liu Yaoting, based on a secret report, immediately led eight team members, including the team leader, to track them down. At 4:00 p.m. on the 19th, Mao, Zhang, and the mastermind Zhang Hanbin were captured in Xugang. They had been rampant in the border area between Jiangsu and Shandong for many years with Liu Guitang. They had been repeatedly suppressed and arrested, but they had always escaped the net. Guangdong Province Actively Promotes Agricultural and Forestry Movement: Gaoyao County Opens New Lingyang Gorge Forest Farm, Heshan County Opens Civilian Reclamation Area, Chaoyang County Can Complete Two Forest Farms This Year 88

Guangzhou Communication: In recent years, Guangdong Province has paid extreme attention to the agricultural and forestry movement. Afforestation and reclamation work in various counties are unusually active. Recently, Ma Bingqian, the head of Gaoyao County, believed that although the various trees planted in the Zhaoqing Gui Ding Mountain Forest Farm were properly planted, the roadsides on both sides still needed to be planted to provide shade for tourists. Yesterday, a special commissioner was sent to the site to plant various trees to enhance the scenery. Also, considering that the area north of Lingyang Gorge is vast, covering hundreds of acres, and can be developed into a forest farm, technicians were sent to survey and draft plans and project proposals. Construction has now begun, and a large number of seedlings, such as tung oil and eucalyptus, have been purchased, hoping to take advantage of the spring rains when plants grow easily. More than one hundred workers have been hired to speed up the work. The Heshan County Government, to help unemployed and impoverished people, has designated Longyan Cave in the Sixth District as the first county-run civilian reclamation area, which has now been opened. It is estimated to accommodate more than 10,000 people. The county government has issued orders to district offices, instructing township heads to clearly investigate the food situation of unemployed impoverished people, list them, and submit reports in order to relocate them to the reclamation area in batches. Furthermore, since the establishment of the Chaoyang County Agricultural and Forestry Promotion Office, it has extensively planted trees. Therefore, the previously barren mountains and desolate lands are now lush with trees and a sight to behold. It has been found that the forest farms that have already been developed include the Xishan County-run Zhongshan Memorial Forest Farm and the Dongyan County-run First Forest Farm. The First Forest Farm is divided into seven forest classes. The second, fourth, fifth, and sixth forest classes were completed last year, and it has been decided that the first, third, and seventh forest classes will also be completed this year. As for the Xishan Forest Farm, which was originally divided into two forest classes, although it was completed last year, the trees in the farm were severely damaged by major and minor typhoons, so replanting will be carried out this year to ensure concealment. In addition, 2,500 acacia trees have been planted along the Huan Cheng Road. In the next few days, 5,000 willow trees will be planted along the river from Shuimen to Houxi Wharf.

Guangdong Province Actively Purchases Silver from Various Affiliated Areas: Special Commissioners Sent to Various Counties to Be Responsible for Absorption; Silver Purchasing Supervisory Office Established 89

Guangzhou Communication: Since the implementation of legal tender in Guangdong Province, the province has been engaged in absorbing silver with legal tender. Recently, the original Japanese fractional coins have disappeared in Guangzhou City. However, various counties are still using paper money (i.e., silver fractional notes of the Provincial and Municipal Banks) to purchase silver as much as possible. The purchasing office is purchasing silver from various villages, and the provincial headquarters has issued orders to various counties and cities, instructing their subordinates to prohibit the direct use of silver. Meanwhile, the Finance Department has telegraphed various counties, sending instructions to county governments, tax revenue agencies, silver purchasing commissioners, tax revenue inspectors, and sub-treasury chiefs, stating roughly that the Provincial Bank has sent staff carrying legal tender to the county to set up offices to purchase silver. It should be announced that from the date of the announcement, all tax revenues and all income from contractors, no matter how much, even less than one yuan, must not accept silver. Violators will be arrested by people's organizations, military and political agencies, and sent to the special court, to be convicted of corruption. The use of silver is also prohibited in market trading and all personnel transactions. Violators on both sides will be punished severely for disrupting financial order. If the delivering party delivers silver, the receiving party should immediately report it and will be rewarded with 80% of the silver delivered. The receiving party should instruct the delivering party to exchange the silver for legal tender at the purchasing office, and the receiving party will still collect the payment from the delivering party separately. The county inspectors should inspect the aforementioned prohibitions at any time. In case of an offender caught in the act, they may immediately arrest and send them to the police. Those who are aware of but fail to report should be punished as accomplices. The Public Security Bureau and district and township offices under the jurisdiction of the county government are responsible for inspection, arrest, and reporting. In addition to submitting separate reports and telegraphing, it is urgent to obey and implement the instructions. The county government immediately recorded the telegraph and announced it on the day of receiving the telegram, and instructed its subordinates to comply with it. It has been found that the most provincial bank purchased about 60 million yuan of silver. Currently, the silver purchased by various staff members in various counties and cities is about 10 million yuan, accounting for about six-tenths of the total silver in the province. The silver received will be stored in silver warehouses built by the Provincial Bank. The number will be transferred to the Legal Tender Issuance Preparatory Management Committee for safekeeping. The Legal Tender Management Committee held a meeting on the 16th to discuss the methods and dates for receiving silver. The candidates for the members of the expert committee and the staff and advisors of the committee have been largely determined. In addition, the Provincial Bank recently established a Silver Purchasing Supervisory Office in conjunction with the Finance Department, which is jointly organized by five members sent by the Finance Department and one member from the Provincial Bank. The responsibilities of the office are to design and supervise the progress of silver purchasing (April 17).

Tang Dynasty Tomb Discovered in Quanzhou: Tomb Bricks Have the Words "Zhenguan Three Years"; Four Tombs Excavated, Yielding Many Ancient Artifacts 90

Xiamen Communication: During the recent expansion of the Zhongshan Park public sports field in Quanzhou City, many ancient tombs were discovered during excavation. It has been confirmed that these are tombs from the Tang Dynasty, but there are no coffins inside, only tomb chambers. When they were discovered, the Jinjiang County Government believed that they had archaeological value and sent a letter to Xiamen University, and the university sent professors Lin Huixiang, Zheng Dekun, and Zhuang Weiji from the School of Arts to supervise the excavation. Initially, a coffin-less tomb was excavated, shaped like a cross. The walls of the tomb were built with ancient bricks engraved with patterns, and the top was like a circular dome with three recessed corners. The tomb pit was 15 feet long, 12 feet 1 inch wide at the shoulder, and 4 feet 10 inches wide at the other end. The bricks were about a foot long, five or six inches wide, and three inches thick. The edges were engraved with patterns of dragons, grass, double fish, turtles, snakes, ancient coins, and six-holed flowers. On the 16th, another tomb was excavated nearby, 4 feet 8 inches deep, and everything was the same as before, but the brick patterns were slightly different. There were words "Suici Yichou" on it. Inside the tomb, there were a broken bottle (amphora-shaped), as well as a bowl-shaped, chamber pot-shaped, candlestick-shaped, lid-shaped, shoe-shaped, and magnetic bottle, one of each, three broken coins, one five-turtle coin, and one large iron nail. On the 17th, two more tombs were excavated, making a total of four. The orientation of all the tombs was northeast to southwest at a 10-degree angle. The first tomb, counting from the east, was only half-excavated because it was quite laborious and was temporarily covered with earth. The second tomb was the one excavated on the 16th. The third tomb was excavated on the 17th and contained ancient bricks, one of which had the four characters "Suici Guiyou". A small round wooden charcoal was also found, and whether it was the charcoal left over from a coffin remains to be studied. The fourth tomb was also excavated on the 17th, and a broken ancient brick was found, with the four characters "Zhenguan Three Years" on it. Connecting it with the "Suici Yichou" character bricks excavated from the second tomb, it can be confirmed that these four tombs are all Tang Dynasty artifacts. Another brick had the words "Intercalary December Fourth," and the following characters were blurred. Inside the fourth tomb, a magnetic plate, five small teacups on the plate (already broken), a magnetic lamp base, and many pieces of broken magnetic bowls were also found. The distance between the first and second tombs is 116 inches, the distance between the second and third tombs is 119 inches, and the distance between the third and fourth tombs is the same. According to Zhuang Weiji, "There are more than ten similar ancient tombs in this area of Zhongshan Park. Four tombs have been excavated, and the unearthed items are now on display for public viewing. When more are excavated in the future, some of the unearthed artifacts will be taken to Xiamen University for research." On the 18th, the first tomb was continued to be excavated. From morning to night, only a quarter was excavated, and a complete round arch door and bones have been discovered. The third tomb was also continued to be excavated, yielding more than 40 kinds of Ming artifacts, including a stove with two pots attached, a , a chamber pot, a spoon, and large and small magnetic bottles. According to Lin Huixiang, it is planned to only excavate these four tombs and not to excavate others, because the unearthed artifacts are sufficient for research (April 19).

Jiangsu Province Anti-Smoking Conference Concludes: Support for Chairman Chiang's Elimination of Opium Addiction 91

Zhenjiang Communication: The Jiangsu Provincial Anti-Smoking Conference continued to hold two or three general meetings on the 21st, chaired in rotation by the three standing committee members of the Provincial Anti-Smoking Association, Leng Yuqiu, Zhou Houjun, and Gu Ziyang. At the morning meeting, the appointed review committee divided all the proposals into four groups for review. In the afternoon, the proposals were discussed one by one based on the review opinions, and the closing ceremony was held. The meeting did not end until 6:00 PM. Provincial Chairman Chen and the provincial party department hosted banquets for the committee members of various counties in the evening. The general meeting resolved the proposals, and the opinions were summarized into the following categories, which are described as follows:

Shorten the Time Limit for Prohibition: Jiangsu Province's anti-smoking limit is four years, starting in May of the 23rd year. Two years have passed. This general meeting decided that if the prohibition in various counties does not require four years in practice, they may request approval from higher authorities to shorten the time limit for prohibition.

Improve the Adjudication of Opium Cases: Regarding the adjudication of opium cases, the counties proposed many opinions for improvement, all advocating that except for special cases, the cases should be tried as soon as they arrive and be completed within a prescribed time limit to avoid backlog. This case is important and will be specially requested by the Provincial Anti-Smoking Association to the provincial government for review and implementation.

Dredge Out Inmates Imprisoned for Opium Offenses: Inmates imprisoned for opium offenses in various county prisons received special support. In addition to the bail measures already stipulated by the provincial government, the general meeting believes that inmates imprisoned for opium should be separated from ordinary inmates and given opportunities to learn skills so that they will not be unemployed after being released from prison. It also advocates for the establishment of more opium addicts factories. Each administrative region should have at least one such facility, implementing military management.

Increase Anti-Smoking Funding: The issue of increasing anti-smoking funding was also the focus of the general meeting's proposal. Therefore, it was resolved to request the provincial government to moderately increase the funding in the provincial budget, and for the anti-smoking associations in various counties to increase the number of investigators and add funding. It was requested that the provincial government implement this in the next year. As for the funding for the anti-smoking departments in various counties, it was advocated that the funding should be determined according to the number of opium addicts and the complexity of the tasks. This should also be implemented in the next year.

Opium Addicts' Treatment Problems: Opium addiction treatment centers in various counties should improve their equipment. Special training should be given for chemical testing techniques, the number of free places should be expanded, and the testing fees should be reduced. After opium addicts quit, they should stay in the treatment center for another week for observation. If opium addicts in various counties evade the treatment, they should be severely punished and prevented from relapsing after quitting. If opium addicts serve as members or staff of public groups, they must be treated in advance.

Opium Paraphernalia Should Be Under Unified Control: The opinions in the proposals are summarized as follows: All opium pipes and lamps originally used by opium-smoking households and opium-selling places must be registered and numbered with the seal of the district office where they are located within a prescribed time limit. All opium pipes and lamps of opium addicts who have been treated and quit must be chemically tested, matched, and burned. Before the end of June of this year, households that do not smoke opium and have opium paraphernalia in stock should report to the district office in charge for destruction. If discovered after the deadline, they will be treated as private opium smokers. The provincial association should send a letter to the provincial government to order the county to quickly implement the "magpie's nest is occupied by the cuckoo" (i.e., confiscate).

Reporting Opium Addicts: Combining everyone's opinions, reporting opium addicts should be handled in accordance with the prescribed procedures. If those who are treated and tested are found to be not addicted, they should be released immediately and should not be detained arbitrarily. The chemical testing fee should be borne by the plaintiff. If they refuse to accept the decision of the opium addiction treatment center and request a re-examination, it should be approved without exception. If the re-examination shows that they are addicted, they should be punished more severely.

Songjiang: Xin Town Chamber of Commerce Must Be Re-elected 92

Half of the members of the first session of the Xin Zhuang Town Chamber of Commerce in the county have completed their terms of office. Therefore, at 9:00 AM on April 20th, the third member representative assembly was convened to re-elect the members in accordance with the law. On that day, 57 member representatives, including Qian Jizhang, attended. Commissioner Xu Zhao of the County Party Department was sent to attend and guide the election. The county government sent Chen Changshan, the head of the third district, as a representative to supervise the election. The presidium reported on the chamber of commerce's affairs and financial status, and discussed and resolved many proposals. Then, the supervisor randomly drew lots in accordance with the law, removing seven executive committee members: Qian Jizhang, Wang Zhaoyun, Shi Jingliang, Cheng Weiru, Pei Siren, Zhang Yigan, and Chen Zhaogen. As for the supervisory committee, since Hu Jingxi had passed away, only Xu Youtang and Zhang Ligen were removed. Immediately after, ballots were issued for the election. As a result, Han Mu Xuan, Xu Youtang, Guan Jichang, Wang Zhaqing, Zhou Baoquan, Cai Jinhua, and Zhu Bingkui were elected as executive committee members with the most votes. Shi Gonghang was elected as chairman of the standing committee. It was also resolved by the general meeting to establish a commercial arbitration office, and nine people, including Zhou Runqi, were elected as councilors. The councilors mutually elected Qian Jizhang as the director of the office.

Suzhou: High Court Investigates the Tragic Case of the Official Slaughter Lane 93

The case of Gu A'gen, an incense seller from the Chen family nunnery in Guan Zai Lane within Lu Gate, being murdered by police officers He Naikang and Hong Shiqin, and patrol captain Zhou of the police district in charge, has resulted in the Wuxian District Court sentencing He Naikang to death and Hong Shiqin and others to various sentences. He Naikang did not accept the judgment and appealed to the High Court. General Mobilization for River Dredging in Rural Areas 95

Various rural areas in Xiyi have received orders to take advantage of the spring agricultural slack season to quickly dredge rivers, and work has already started separately. Details are as follows: The Yang Yuan River in the Tenth District was previously estimated for the project by the Construction Bureau, and the deadline for dredging was set. However, due to the large size of the dam construction project, work has not yet started. Now, in accordance with the provincial labor service regulations, the county government has ordered Assistant Zhou Yeping from the district to work with Qian Nianwen, the head of Yangshuyuan Town, and Kuang Bo'an, the head of Kuangqiao Township, to supervise the work, which has now started. The Zhang Miao She River in Zhang Miao She Township in the Sixth District has been decided to be dredged by the village chief meeting. The work is divided into sections, and the first section is from Xihutang Bankou to Nanheng River, which is 2 kilometers long and has more than 40,000 cubic meters of earthwork. Work started the day before yesterday.

Changshu: Rice Mill Workers Camp Out to Petition 96

Last year, the Runfeng Rice Mill in this county dismissed four workers, including Zhang Yinchang. The labor union believed that they were dismissed without reason, and a dispute arose between labor and management. It has been more than eight months since then, and the labor's demand for the factory to continue employing them has not been resolved. Strikes and petitions have occurred repeatedly. Now, the Central Ministry of Industry and Commerce has approved that the dismissed workers should be reinstated in accordance with the Trade Union Law. However, the management also handles the matter according to the Factory Law of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, resulting in prolonged unresolved situation. On the 20th of this month, the rice mill workers stopped working again and gathered to petition both the party and the government, demanding the implementation of the arbitration agreement. At that time, the county secretary went to Wuxi for a meeting, and the section chief was unwilling to take responsibility, causing the petitioning workers to gather and wait for the secretary to return to Changshu for implementation. In the evening, the workers camped out to wait for a resolution. Various labor unions learned about the situation, and people such as rickshaw pullers and barbers bought bread and other food to console them. However, the rice hall stated that the workers were pulled away by Zhang Yinchang and others to strike without reason, causing the hall to be shut down and resulting in heavy losses. They have informed the labor union that if the workers do not return to work in the hall on the 21st, they will be considered to have resigned automatically. As a result, the gap between labor and management is widening, and it is difficult to resolve the situation for the time being.

Gaoyou: Farmers in Shi Zhuang Township Robbed by Bandits 97

The farm household of Zhu Kaitong, located about three miles northeast of Shi Zhuang Township in the sixth district of this county, is quite wealthy, which attracted the attention of bandits. At about 1:00 AM last night (the 18th), more than a dozen bandits, each carrying guns, knives, and flashlights, broke into the house, waking up the family members. They searched everywhere and only found more than one hundred yuan in cash and jewelry and clothing worth about two hundred yuan, which was not enough to satisfy them. They then tied up Zhu himself with ropes, beat him severely, forced him to hand over the hidden silver, and used fire to burn his armpits. Zhu could not bear the pain and said that there was one hundred yuan in cash under the stove. The bandits went to get it as he said and then fled with the loot. The total loss is estimated at more than four hundred yuan.

Haimen: Park Takes Initial Shape 98

Chen Guiqing, the magistrate of Haimen County, recognizing that the county seat is a densely populated area lacking a proper public recreational area, purchased more than ten mu of private land north of the old West Garden to develop a park. The budget is 5,000 yuan, which was approved by the Construction Department to be used from the county's reserve fund. The preliminary shape of the park is now taking shape, and various flowers and trees have been planted. The Construction Section is currently drafting plans for the pavilions and bridges to be built and will start construction. In addition, Gu Shaoqing, the general manager of the Shanghai Huacheng Tobacco Company, and squire Wang Yijing, both natives of the county, each donated 500 yuan to build two pavilions. The plans were drafted by the design committee member Lu Qinmin, and construction is scheduled to begin on the first day of next month.

Cinders Added to Highway 99

There are a total of seventeen main roads in Haimen County. They have been in disrepair for years, and the road surface is uneven. The county government has long planned to add cinders and prepared a budget, which was submitted to the Construction Department for approval last winter. The instruction was received that the plan was feasible, but before the Puqi Highway is built, the route may be changed, so it seems unnecessary to add cinders first, and it is difficult to approve. Last month, Gu Shiyi, a technician from the Construction Department, and Zhao Zuzhang, a resident engineer from Nantong, came to Haimen to inspect the road construction. Both believed that it was necessary to expedite the repairs. After receiving the instruction, Section Chief Jiang first added cinders to the section connecting Nantong to the county seat, which is more than 20 li long. The cinders needed were all supplied by the three factories, and the cars were used for loading and transportation. The project can be completed within days. Section Chief Jiang is currently drafting a plan to add cinders to all the main roads in the county. The budget plan was delivered to technician Wang Jie yesterday for drafting, and it will be submitted to the department for approval and implementation as soon as it is drafted.

Nantong: Commemorate National Hero Cao Ding 100

During the Jiajing reign of the Ming Dynasty, Cao Ding, a native of the county, raised troops to resist foreign invaders and died in Pingchao. The six counties under Nantong have now raised 30,000 yuan to build a special ancestral hall to commemorate him. It has been surveyed to be located on a hundred mu of farmland west of the Nan Baitang Temple. On the 20th, Special Commissioner Ge reported to all sectors of society that the original plan had been changed. In addition to building an auditorium to house the portrait, a large-scale review ground will be built, as well as camp classrooms, for the team students in the district to practice their skills. He has requested instructions from the province on how to proceed.

Four freight cars have been allocated, and office member Wang Yanling has been dispatched to prepare together with station staff and drivers. The freight will still be collected according to the usual rates and will not be increased.

The lantern parade for banning opium and rejecting drugs in this city is held on April 26th according to the provisions of Article 3 of the implementation plan of the preparatory committee. Name; 2. Position; 3. Number of representatives; 4. Name of representative organization; 5. Seal of the person in charge of the organization; 6. Seal of the organization; 7. Date of submission. The flags for the commander, deputy commander, chief marshal, and deputy marshal will be distributed by the preparatory committee. Each group provides its own symbols. Participants from each group must pay attention to neatness and cleanliness. The commander and chief marshal of the City Party Headquarters and the Public Security Bureau will be the ones issuing orders. The commanders and marshals of other organizations must absolutely obey. The slogans for the lantern parade will be distributed by the committee to the commanders and marshals to lead and shout. Marchers must strictly observe order. If reactionary elements are found to be mixed in to make trouble, they should immediately be handed over to the military police for legal action. Organizations participating in the lantern parade should provide their own lamps and candles, and each should prepare a large lamp representing the organization for identification. The slogans used on the lamps should follow the regulations of the committee, and the style of the lamps must be uniform. Lanterns that are meaningless, such as clam shells and "swinging river boats," are prohibited from participating. Organizations participating in the lantern parade must gather at the Ximen Public Gymnasium at 5:30 PM on the 26th to await departure. The order of the lantern parade is as follows: 1. Military Band of the Headquarters; 2. City Party Headquarters; 3. Municipal Government and affiliated agencies; 4. Military Band and Police of the Public Security Bureau; 5. City Farmers Association; 6. General Labor Union; 7. City Chamber of Commerce; 8. City Education Association and Students; 9. Boy Scouts Military Band; 10. Boy Scouts; 11. Citizens' Federation; 12. Others; 13. Defense Corps.

Lantern Parade Route: On the 26th (Sunday) at 5:00 PM, gather at the Public Gymnasium on Dajilu, Xiejiao. Li Shizeng Returned to Shanghai Yesterday Afternoon 103

Central Committee member Li Shizeng traveled to Europe and America at the end of last year. He returned to Shanghai yesterday at 12:30 PM aboard the Empress of Japan, a ship of the Chang & Co. Upon arrival, former Minister of Justice and Administration Wei Daoming, Xiao Jinfang representing Central Committee member Wang Chonghui, Li's secretary Li Xixian, and friends Pang Zanchen, Chen Mengzhao, Qi Yunqing, and others went to the ship to welcome him. Li met with reporters from the Xin Sheng News Agency on the ship and made the following remarks:

The Journey: Li first said, "Due to international cultural affairs, I must go abroad once a year to make contacts. This time, I departed in December last year and first went to the United States to carry out the establishment of an international library in New York. Then, I crossed the Atlantic to Europe, visited the Chinese International Libraries in Geneva and Paris, Switzerland and France, and then crossed the Atlantic again, taking a ship from Canada back to China. This trip lasted four months. Besides the aforementioned tasks, there were no other missions."

European Situation: Li then answered reporters' questions, saying, "The world situation is changing rapidly. One does not know what will happen tomorrow. For example, regarding the situation in Europe, one or two days before the German army entered the Rhineland, I was in Strasbourg, France, visiting the largest printing house in France. The bureau specializes in the publication of large dictionaries and encyclopedias, which are world-famous. Unexpectedly, only a few dozen hours after I left the place, this sudden incident occurred. As for what will happen in the future, whether this will lead to a major war, I dare not say."

Unity Issue: The reporter then raised the issue of the sincere unity that all parties are currently working for and asked Li for his opinion. According to his answer, "I have been abroad for months and am not yet clear about the domestic situation. This matter is a long story. I feel like asking 'where to begin talking about the Twenty-Four Histories.' Now that Mr. Hu Zhantang has returned to China, when I arrived in Europe, Mr. Hu had already left Europe, and I did not get to meet him. This time I returned to China by ship from America, and I was unable to go through the ports of Hong Kong and Guangdong, so I did not get to meet him either. After arriving in Shanghai, I will visit Mr. Wang Liangchou. I will also have to go to Nanjing to visit President Jiang and others to catch up."
