Yu Qiaqing and Others Submit Suggestions on Moving Graves to the Zhejiang Provincial Government: Public Cemetery First, Then Order the People to Move 108

Strive for Prudence and Avoid Haste During the Transition Period. Yu Qiaqing and others from the Ningbo Association in Shanghai believe that the Yinxian government's demolition and relocation of graves in the market towns is not being handled according to procedures, causing unrest among the villagers. They have proposed three measures and submitted them to the Chairman of the Zhejiang Provincial Government for adoption in order to show compassion. The original submission stated: "We humbly submit that our association recently learned that the demolition and relocation of graves in various townships under the jurisdiction of Ji (Ningbo) is being handled hastily, causing overseas compatriots to protest. In addition, the Yinxian government recently announced that all existing floating coffins and exposed coffins in the old urban area must be demolished by the 15th of May. The villagers are extremely anxious after hearing the news. We have already submitted a request to your office on the 9th to correct this matter. We received a reply from your office, showing your Excellency's utmost concern for the people. We admire you immensely. We have investigated that Yinci counties are handling this case without following procedures and without considering the situation, causing unrest among the villagers. This is a dispute in Ningbo that has not occurred in recent years. Based on our limited perspective, we believe that there are several aspects that should be corrected, and we respectfully present them to your Excellency. The first is the procedural issue. Moving graves must first have a public cemetery as a place for them to be relocated. This way, the graves being moved will not have nowhere to go. Now, let us ask how many townships have already established public cemeteries, and what is the capacity of the existing public cemeteries? The county government has not yet unified them, and it is difficult for each township to popularize them. However, those in charge disregard the facts and focus solely on registration and urging relocation. The people do not know what to do, leading to complaints. In recent times, the graves that have been forced to be relocated have had no choice but to be moved into the mountains. The price of mountain land has soared, and the work of building graves has become busy. The cost of moving one grave is at least over one hundred gold. If they still need to be moved into the public cemetery in the future, they will inevitably fall into double the labor and expense. If we put ourselves in their shoes, how many can not complain? For the government's sake, it is advisable to urge the townships to concentrate their efforts on establishing public cemeteries. When the public cemeteries are completed, then demand that the people relocate, so that things can be fair and the resentment can be eliminated. This concerns the handling

Two Railway Lines and Eurasia Company to Handle Joint Road-Air Passenger Transport; Agreement Negotiated and Now Being Signed; to be Implemented on the First of Next Month 109

The Jinghu and Huhangyong Railway Bureaus and the Eurasia Aviation Company, in order to facilitate passengers and develop domestic joint transportation, have agreed to handle road-air joint transportation. Personnel from the Transportation Department of the Railway Bureau and the Operations Group of the Company have been negotiating for a long time and have reached an agreement on the joint transportation methods and drafted a contract of seventeen articles, which is currently being signed by both parties. The transfer stations are designated as Shanghai and Nanjing, and major stations along the road and along the line are designated as joint transportation stations. All procedures are now ready, and it is scheduled to be implemented on May 1st, with a trial period of one year. After the expiration, the contract will be revised with the consent of both parties. The original text of the contract has been found and recorded below:

Designated Joint Transportation Stations

The Jinghu and Huhangyong Railway Administration (hereinafter referred to as the Railway Bureau) and the Eurasia Aviation Company (hereinafter referred to as the Company), in order to facilitate passengers and assist in the development of road-air joint transportation business, have specially signed this road-air passenger joint transportation contract. The terms and conditions are as follows: 1. Both parties agree to sell road-air passenger joint transportation tickets at the joint transportation stations. The Railway Bureau designates Shanghai North Station, Suzhou, Wuxi, Changzhou, Zhenjiang, and Jiaxing and Hangzhou as joint transportation stations. The Company designates Shanghai, Nanjing, Zhengzhou, Xi'an, Chengdu, Kunming, Beiping, Lanzhou, Ningxia, and Baotou as joint transportation stations. Both parties also designate Shanghai and Nanjing as transfer stations. 2. When the Railway Bureau has passengers who want to purchase road-air joint transportation tickets, it should first inquire with the Company whether there are seats available. Only after the Company approves can the tickets be sold. When the Company sells joint transportation tickets, if the passenger needs to reserve a seat or sleeper, it must first inquire with the Railway Bureau whether there are seats or berths available. Only after the Railway Bureau approves can the tickets be sold. After the said tickets are sold, the Railway Bureau or the Company should immediately send the seat reservation form to the other party for reference.

Ticket Grade

3. The grade of joint transportation tickets is limited to first class within the scope of the Railway Bureau. Within the scope of the Company, there is no distinction in grade. 4. The Railway Bureau or the Company shall obtain its printed train timetable or flight timetable, as well as various regulations regarding passengers, and send them to each station and airline of the other party at any time. Either party, upon receiving the above items, shall immediately arrange for them to be placed in a conspicuous location and published in various publications designated by both parties to promote road-air joint transportation in order to expand publicity. 5. The ticket prices of the Railway Bureau and the Company will be listed in a separate table attached later. The table is also part of the contract. 6. Joint transportation passengers, when taking trains or planes at Shanghai and Nanjing transfer stations, the joint transportation of vehicles for pick-up and drop-off from the station to the airport or from the airport to the station shall be borne by the passengers themselves. 7. The style of the joint transportation tickets shall be printed and issued by the Railway Bureau after consultation with the Company. The printing cost shall be borne by the Railway Bureau if the tickets are sold by the Railway Bureau, and by the Company if the tickets are sold by the Company.

Refund Procedures

8. If a passenger, after purchasing a joint transportation ticket, stops the journey due to some reason, the purchased ticket should be submitted to the departure station of the Railway Bureau or the Company or the station where the journey is stopped for visa at least thirty-six hours before the designated flight or two hours before the train departs. The ticket refund can only be processed at 90% of the ticket price. The ticket will be collected and invalidated. The 10% handling fee deducted shall be earned by the Railway Bureau or the Company that sold the ticket. If the Railway Bureau or the Company encounters the above situation, it should immediately notify the other party to avoid wasting seats and incurring intangible losses. 9. If the Railway Bureau or the Company encounters a train or plane stopping or being unable to proceed midway, or for other reasons, it needs to cancel the passenger's seat or berth and return all or part of the joint transportation fare to the passenger, the passenger should submit the relevant ticket to the departure station of the Railway Bureau or the Company or the station where the journey is stopped for visa. Then, the Railway Bureau or the Company will refund all or part of the ticket price to the passenger and invalidate the original ticket. 10. The inquiry method stipulated in Article 2, for the Railway Bureau and the Company's transfer stations, both parties may inquire nearby. If one party does not have a transfer station, the other party may notify the transfer station by telegram or telephone for inquiry, depending on the situation.

Settlement of Joint Transportation Fees

11. Joint transportation ticket fees will be settled once a month. Before the 10th of each month, the joint transportation statements of each camp for the previous month (such as ticket sales statements and ticket refund statements) shall be exchanged between the two parties for detailed verification. The accounting department of the Railway Bureau shall prepare a settlement list and hand it over to the Company clearly on the 24th of the same month. 12. The tickets sold or collected by both parties, together with the canceled tickets, should be reported to each other on a monthly basis for verification. 13. Matters within the scope of air transportation that are not covered by this contract shall be handled in accordance with the mutual transportation regulations. Matters within the scope of road transportation that are not covered by this contract shall be handled in accordance with the road transportation regulations. 14. Joint transportation tickets will not be sold to children under the age of 16 who are not accompanied by a guardian. 15. When selling road-air joint transportation tickets, ticket sellers from both parties must have the passenger declare that, when boarding the plane, they should personally sign under the abstract of the Company's passenger regulations on the back of the joint transportation ticket and hand it over to the person in charge of the airport for safekeeping.

Contract Period of One Year

16. This platform will be in the same format from May 1, 1936 to April 30, 1937, with a one-year trial period. If both parties are willing to continue, they should notify each other in person one month before the expiration date. 17. If there are any matters not covered by this contract, the other party may be notified in writing one month in advance to negotiate revisions.

Both Parties Are Signing

Attached are the prices of various departments of the two roads and airlines, all of which have been corrected into three identical copies. The operations group director of Eurasia Aviation Company, Liao Guanxuan, is signing them and submitting them to General Manager Li Jing for approval. Then, a letter will be sent to the Railway Bureau, signed by the head of the transportation department, Xiao Weiguo, deputy director Liu Dingxin, and Wang Zhigang, and submitted to Director Huang Boqiao and Deputy Director Wu Shaozeng for approval before taking effect. Each party shall hold one copy as proof. However, the company stated regarding the provisions of Article 8 that no refunds may be requested at intermediate stations during air travel and has notified the Railway Bureau. As for the passenger ticket, the format has also been determined, with a total of five copies. In addition to the stub retained by the passenger, the first and second copies will be collected for verification when boarding the plane and alighting from the train. The third copy is the regular ticket, with the child ticket attached. Note 1: It will be collected upon arrival at the destination station. Each copy details the departure and arrival stations and the transfer station designated by the passenger. There is also an abstract of the company's regulations attached for passengers to consult. The procedures that need to be corrected are also described. 1. Regarding the area issue, the current demolition and relocation of graves is not based on the county as a unit, but on the township or town as a unit. Often, township A has already carried out the relocation, while town B still allows new construction. Within the same county, there is this extreme contradictory situation. The people clearly observe and listen, but cannot decide whether to comply. The names and areas of townships and towns have been repeatedly changed in recent years, sometimes dividing the whole into parts, and sometimes merging B into A. Villagers live in their place but do not know the name of their township or town. Moreover, those who are buried here are not necessarily people from their township or town. Those who are from different townships, different towns, or different counties, and who are distant guests from other places, are also often found. If the township or town head urges registration and relocation every day, even though announcements have been issued and advertisements have been placed, it is already difficult to expect people to know about it through local newspapers that are only sold in Ningbo Port and announcements posted in one town or township. In addition, the names and areas of their townships and towns are not fully understood by the people, so the effectiveness of the announcement can be said to be equal to zero. If people are blamed for not registering on time, and if demolition and relocation are carried out when they do not register, and the entrusted person is not the right person, the supervision may not be perfect, and opportunities are taken to engage in personal gain. Bad people take the opportunity to allude, and there are those who are suddenly discovered without being designated by the township or town office. There are those who impersonate the township or town office and extort money. According to reports from villagers, the recent demolition of graves in the eastern part of Yinxian County focuses on the large and intact ones, while the dilapidated and exposed coffins are given a slow treatment. What is the intention? It is not necessary to ask. What crime have the villagers committed to suffer such trampling? Tracing back to the reason, it is because the township is self-governing, which is extremely harmful. It is advisable for the county government to handle it in a unified manner according to the regulations, and at the same time, clearly announce the registration deadline and publish it in various newspapers in Shanghai so that everyone can know it, so that all those who have graves in the county know where the rules are and there will be no ambiguity in the measures, so as to avoid being excavated due to misunderstanding. This concerns the area of handling that should be corrected. The second is the time issue. According to Ningbo customs, grave sacrifices are usually held during Qingming. It is rare to go to the countryside to sacrifice to graves at other times. Townships and towns often arbitrarily set the deadline for registering graves, sometimes setting it in March or May, extending it for one or two months, and then closing it immediately. It is not easy to make the general public aware of the opportunity unless it happens to be during the Qingming sacrifice period. It is advisable to set a generous deadline so that people can register as much as possible. The registration period should start before Qingming of the previous year and end after Qingming of the next year. Those who still have not registered according to the regulations after two sweeping and sacrificing periods should be designated as ownerless graves, so as to avoid the suspicion of arbitrary decisions. This concerns the handling of time that should be corrected. 3. Summarizing the above three points, they are all the shortcomings of the current handling. Unless they are corrected one by one, it will be difficult to eliminate the disturbances and facilitate the promotion. Some argue that the current disturbances are due to the poor burial system in the past, which is true. However, reforming the old system also has its own gradual process and a considerable period of time. The ancients have warned us that haste makes waste. Everyone secretly discusses and believes that moving floating graves and limiting the future are appropriate ways to deal with filling graves at present. Going beyond this limit involves complexity and harshness. Our fellow villager Committee Member Jiang Weifang will govern the world with filial piety. Reports on the relocation of graves in Guangdong Province have been repeatedly seen in newspapers and spread among the villagers as a good story. We believe that the government officials should admire the meaning of the Chairman's intention and promote his benevolence to all kinds. When handling this case, we must strive for prudence and avoid haste. Who is not a child of man? Who does not have ancestral graves? When one thinks of this, how can one not be fearful? If one manages this matter with utmost care, there is nothing that will not be done with even more care. If this is the way the world is influenced, the morals of the people will return to generosity, and the governance will become prosperous. Due to the previous reasons, we have gathered the public opinion of the villagers and presented our humble opinions. We humbly request your office to adopt them and order the counties under the jurisdiction of Old Ningbo to implement them. We cannot wait anxiously. Ningbo Association in Shanghai, Yu Qiaqing and others respectfully submit to the Chairman of the Zhejiang Provincial Government.

The Shanghai County Government issued an order to establish township and town cemeteries and ordered the districts to follow the regulations. It is heard that Minhang and Zhuanqiao and other places have plans to prepare for construction. Yesterday, the county government also instructed the district chiefs, stating that for prosperous towns and cities or villages with mostly rice fields that are not suitable for building graves, appropriate areas should be found in other nearby townships and towns for construction. As for mountains and barren land, if the property rights are privately owned, they can be requisitioned according to law.

Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Continues to Petition for the Tea Industry 111

If the Anhui Provincial Government Does Not Accept the Tea Industry's Request, All Tea Firms Will Suspend Business from Tomorrow 112

Requesting the Municipal Government to Telegraph Anhui Province to Seek Maintenance 113

Due to the Yangzhuang tea firms' inability to operate because the Anhui Provincial Government is controlling Qimen tea, the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce resolved to suspend foreign exchange transactions. The Chamber persuaded them to postpone the suspension for two days, implementing it from the 23rd. Meanwhile, it telegraphed the Anhui Provincial Government, requesting the adoption of the tea industry's demands, as reported in yesterday's newspaper. It is now learned that the Chamber received a telegraph from the Provincial Government yesterday, and urgently telegraphed the Shanghai Municipality, and submitted another petition to the Shanghai Municipal Government, requesting the telegraphing of the Anhui Provincial Government to order the retraction of loans. Special inquiries reveal the following telegrams:

Anhui Provincial Government Telegram

The Anhui Provincial Government telegraphed a reply to Yu Qiaqing, stating: "To Mr. Yu Qiaqing, Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, your kind telegram has been received. The improvement of black tea transportation and sales in both provinces takes into account both tea farmers and tea merchants. If the tea firms in Shanghai can fully accept and implement the points mentioned in the telegram, it would be most appropriate. The submission from the association, delivered only recently, contains many discrepancies compared to what the representatives negotiated in the province. Instructions have been given to proceed according to the telegram. We hope for your strong and sincere persuasion to benefit the tea industry. Anhui Provincial Government Chairman Liu Zhenhua, with seal."

Chamber of Commerce Urgent Telegram: The Municipal Chamber of Commerce urgently telegraphed the Anhui Provincial Government in Anqing, stating: "Your Excellency, Anhui Provincial Government, your telegram has been received. We have just received a statement from all tea firm merchants, stating that the Anhui Provincial Government's reply to Mr. Yu Qiaqing instructs our Chamber to fully accept the points mentioned in the telegram. We have investigated and found that the True Telegram is subject to the supervision and direction of the transportation and sales office, which is completely obstructed according to reason and cannot be followed. We intend to adhere to the requests in the submission on the first day of the month, where each firm will set up a sales office, open a report of the tea market daily, and submit it to the transportation and sales office. Upon arrival of the tea, the transportation and sales office will immediately send the bill of lading to the sales office jointly formed by the tea firms, so that there is capital turnover. Other methods shall be in accordance with the submission on the first day of the month. After investigating the submission on the first day of the month and what the representatives proposed in the province, there are only four points added, and the rest are completely the same. We implore you to show compliance. All tea firms in our Chamber stretch their necks and stand on tiptoe, waiting for your final orders, otherwise they will inevitably walk into the dead end of suspending foreign exchange transactions and closing their businesses on the 23rd." An investigation reveals that the industry's proposal to open a report of the tea market daily is under the supervision of the transportation and sales office, which is what our Chamber's telegram means by following the True Telegram and handling it in a compromise manner. In addition, the points listed in the original submission of the Chamber members, according to reports, are the same as the face-to-face negotiations in the province. We implore your Excellency to consider the tea firms, which are a Chinese export industry with a long history, and show extraordinary compassion to fully preserve the foundation and avoid sudden changes. The tea industry is following the persuasion of our Chamber to postpone the suspension of foreign exchange transactions and business closures from the 23rd. If, before the deadline, we do not obtain your Excellency's order to adopt the telegram, the suspension of foreign exchange transactions must be implemented, which will inevitably increase commercial panic and affect finance. The situation is urgent. Awaiting your telegram reply. Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, respectfully."

Tomorrow's Suspension of Foreign Exchange Transactions: A reporter from the New Voice Society obtained definite news from the Yangzhuang Tea Industry Association yesterday that the tea firms' resolution to suspend foreign exchange transactions is actually for the sake of fighting for survival. The Chamber of Commerce is currently strongly persuading them to postpone it for two days, implementing it from the 23rd. If the Anhui Provincial Government is unwilling to be understanding and accepting, then the tea firms will have no business to operate and will have no choice but to suspend the exchange of bills and announce it to the people in order to seek public judgment, it is said.

Telegram to the Municipal Government

"To His Excellency, the Shanghai Municipal Government, on the 20th of this month, according to a letter from the Shanghai Yangzhuang Tea Industry Association, it states: 'Our association previously stated that the Anhui Provincial Government planned to control the transportation and sale of black tea, which hindered business. Earlier, a telegram from Dong expressly promised not to hinder the tea firms' lending, but now goes back on their word, which is tantamount to trapping people in a pit. We have repeatedly asked your esteemed association to telegraph the Anhui Provincial Government to request exemption from discussion in order to relieve commercial difficulties. At the same time, we sent Sun Xiquan, etc., to Anhui to petition, and they have stated the position of the tea firms, the situation of lending, and all opinions to Yang, the Director of the Department of Finance, and Liu, the Director of the Department of Construction, reasonably. The representatives also took into account the government's credibility and the merchants' business, and under the circumstances of considering both sides, they drafted a compromise method and presented the draft, sincerely discussing it. Subsequently, Chen, the secretary of the competent department, and others informed them that if they could obtain the consent of the industry when they returned to Shanghai and submit a revised formal presentation, they would approve the telegram reply. This government need not lend separately, etc.' Our association then submitted this presentation on the first day of the month by post, and it was also sent by Hong Mengpan, Chen Yizhou, and others, and your esteemed association repeatedly re-telegraphed the situation in the case. Since the opening of trade, the position of the tea firms and the freedom of the people to operate businesses should be protected by law. Even if we discuss this year's lending, it was because we received a reply from the Anhui Provincial Government in advance that it would not hinder it, that we actively raised funds and invested. If the Anhui Provincial Government is not forgetful, it should clearly know that the tea firms' business starts with lending and ends with sales, which is a consistent commercial practice that cannot be analyzed separately. It is inappropriate to explicitly promise in advance and then discuss the method of controlling transportation and sales later, using the excuse of revitalizing the tea industry to exhaust the profits of merchants. Therefore, from our association's perspective, even if we insist on maintaining the original business model unchanged, it would be legally justified and logically reasonable. Moreover, the aforementioned compromise method has indeed sought a compromise. Because we saw that the tea season was approaching and time was pressing, we did not want to suspend the case indefinitely, causing long-term disturbances, leading to disadvantages for tea merchants and farmers, and taking into account the overall situation with great pains. We were waiting for a reply, but unexpectedly, the Anhui Provincial Government did not issue it and instead proceeded with lending in the Qimen production area to the tea houses that had already received firm loans, which shows that they have gone back on their word repeatedly and are attempting to fulfill their exclusive desires. There is no need to conceal that they are operating a provincial monopoly. Such deliberate destruction will not only make it impossible for the tea firms' business to continue in the future, but also cause the current millions of loans to be on the verge of falling through. Under the circumstances where black tea is being sacrificed, green tea has no more energy to take care of it. Bankruptcy and collapse are imminent. At this time when all industries are sluggish and the market is very depressed, what impact will the tea industry have on the producing provinces if it is allowed to decline? We will not discuss it for the time being. However, if the tea firms in this city, which occupy an important position, all perish, then the disastrous impression that will affect the entire city will be unbearable. Our association, in view of the seriousness of the situation, has not only stopped the release of all black tea loans and waited quietly for a solution, but also corresponded to your esteemed association, requesting you to quickly present the case to the Shanghai Municipal Government to appeal for relief and immediately telegraph the Anhui Provincial Government for strict negotiations to maintain business and protect the market. Based on this, after the news of the Qimen tea control was published in the newspapers, the association repeatedly sent letters to the industry association to request rescue. After receiving a letter from the National Economic Committee, it replied that the purpose of the previous tea technology discussion meeting was to improve Chinese tea and there was no matter of controlling Qimen tea. The transportation and sales method is still under careful study and will not hinder the tea firms' lending, etc. Now the Anhui authorities have gone back on their word, and the four compromise methods presented by the three representatives of the industry have not been approved. In the Qimen production area, loans are being implemented to the tea houses that have already received firm loans. The industry was alarmed upon hearing the news and convened an emergency meeting of the industry on the 19th of this month, resolving to stop the release of all red and green tea loans. The association, in view of the urgency of the situation, advised the industry to postpone the aforementioned resolution for two days and urgently telegraph the competent authorities to telegraph a fair solution. We hereby submit this matter to your honorable government for observation, and request your honorable government to telegraph the Anhui Provincial Government, instructing the Black Tea Transportation and Sales Association to retract the loans from the tea houses that have already received firm loans. On the one hand, we instruct them to follow the four compromise methods presented by the three representatives, so as to maintain the dwindling life of the tea firms, which is for the public good. Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, respectfully."

New Japanese Military Attaché, Kita Seiichi, Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday 115

The newly appointed Army Military Attaché to the Japanese Embassy in China, Kita Seiichi, came to China to take up his new post. He arrived in Shanghai at 3:40 PM yesterday, accompanied by his wife and daughter, on the Japanese ship Asama Maru. The ship docked at the Huishan Wharf. Wang Changchun, a commissioner of the Shanghai Municipal Government, Zhou Jue, the director of the Diplomatic Ministry's Shanghai Office, and Wakasugi, a councilor of the Japanese Embassy in China, Ishishe, the consul-general in Shanghai, Ueda, the head of the police corps, Utsunomiya, the military attaché stationed in Beijing, Sakamoto, and dozens of representatives of Japanese residents in Shanghai welcomed him at the port. After greeting each welcoming person, Kita met with Chinese and Japanese newspaper reporters. According to him, the rumors that he would convene a meeting of military attachés stationed in China after taking office are not true. As for the Japanese military's plan to increase the number of troops stationed in North China, as of today, not a single soldier has been added. It has not yet been decided when he will go to Beijing to pay respects to the Chinese authorities. It is also a misunderstanding that he will go to Southern China, he said.

A Telecommunications Agency dispatch from Tokyo on the 21st reported: "The military authorities believe that the attitude of the National Government and the situation in North China are not optimistic. After Kita, the military attaché stationed in China, who is currently on his way to take office, inspects the local situation, a major meeting will be held in Qingdao around June, gathering military attachés stationed in various parts of China. The central government will also send powerful officials concerned to China to comprehensively review China policy, especially relations with the Soviet Union, focusing on the results of Kita's military attaché's inspection and reports from local military attachés, and comprehensively review China's policy towards Japan and the Soviet Union in order to establish a concrete plan for implementing continental policy, and advance in the same direction as the military streamlining and national administration reform currently underway."

Bankers Association Establishes Bankers' Business Mutual Benefit Association 119

Daily Meetings Will Be Held Starting on the 1st 120

Since the government's new currency system policy and the unrestricted buying and selling of foreign exchange by the Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications were implemented, the foreign exchange market rate is announced daily by the Central Bank, and domestic exchange has become balanced. The Shanghai Bankers Association's previous Market Rate Committee is no longer necessary and was immediately disbanded. Now, in order to improve their business, the banks have decided to reorganize the Market Rate Committee into a Bankers' Business Mutual Benefit Association, which belongs to the same industry association as the Bankers' Society.

Establishment Purpose: The association's articles of association have been approved by the eighth executive committee meeting of the Bankers Association. Its purpose is: A. To connect the friendship of colleagues and to facilitate the handover of affairs in the same industry. B. To assist each other in studying all the main issues in business. C. To investigate the financial market conditions and visit various industries. Members are divided into basic members and proficient members. All member banks of the Bankers Association are basic members. All non-member banks of the Bankers Association are ordinary members, and a committee is established to preside over it.

Prior Meetings: In addition to the member banks of the Bankers Association joining as basic members, the Central Bank and other banks have joined as ordinary members. It is stipulated that at 10:00 AM every day, each bank should send one representative to gather at the Bankers Association meeting (except Sundays and holidays), report on the financial market conditions in various ports to each other, and study the improvement of business. Now each bank has sent personnel (i.e., the former Market Rate Committee representatives) to the Bankers Association meeting for about one hour starting on April 1st, and a check-in book is prepared for the representatives to sign.

Further General Meeting: The association has decided to hold a general meeting in the near future to elect a committee of about 15 members and elect one chairman and one vice-chairman to preside over everything. If there are opinions on improving banking business, they will be submitted to the association's executive committee for handling after being approved by the association. In the future, it will be decided to solicit various non-member banks to join as ordinary members, and various rules are being drafted by the association.

Mining Association Requests Reduction of Mining Tax 121

More Than 30 Copies of Mining Survey Forms Have Been Received 122

It Will Be Submitted to the Ministry of Industry after Procedures Are Completed 123

The China Mining Association believes that foreign coal is being dumped in China, and domestic coal is inconvenient to transport and the mining tax is too high, making it difficult to compete with foreign coal. In order to save the situation, the representatives of all members decided at a general meeting to submit a petition to the Ministry of Industry to transfer it to the Ministry of Finance for a reduction of the mining tax. After receiving the Ministry's instructions, they were instructed to fill in the actual annual output, sales price, and exact amount of mining tax of each mine in detail and report them in order to verify and transfer them, etc. The association immediately formulated forms and distributed them to various mines. More than 30 detailed forms filled out by the Six River Gulch and North China mines have been received one after another. They are currently being reviewed separately. After completing the procedures, they will be submitted to the Ministry of Industry and the details of each mine will be reported to request the Ministry of Finance to reduce the mining tax again in order to reduce costs, fight against foreign coal, prevent leaks, and benefit the mining industry.

Skin Thread Tobacco Association Submits to the Tax Bureau: Requesting Prohibition of Special Tax on Fujian Tobacco Threads; Tobacco Threads are Made with Ingredients, Cannot be Taxed the Same as Tobacco Leaves 126

The Shanghai Skin Thread Tobacco Association, due to the Fujian Tingzhou Tax Collection Bureau's unauthorized addition of a special tax on tobacco threads, has specially submitted a request to the Tax Bureau, requesting a prohibition. The original text reads: "Submitting a request regarding the Fujian Tingzhou Tobacco and Alcohol Tax Collection Bureau's unauthorized addition of a special tax on tobacco threads, which is demanding and distorting, violating established cases, coercing and obstructing, hindering freight transport, earnestly requesting strict prohibition to alleviate merchants' difficulties and maintain regulations."

"According to reports from fellow businesses in Minnan and Yongding, the Fujian Tingzhou Tobacco and Alcohol Tax Collection Bureau, using the excuse of untaxed tobacco threads, has decided to implement a presumed tax increase from April 1st of this year. Fearing that the increase would be insufficient, they have also ordered the provision of a guarantee bond, holding them responsible for supplementary payments. Tobacco merchants cannot bear the burden, and goods cannot be shipped out, resulting in obstruction and coercion. Both domestic and foreign merchants are deeply angered and have requested the association to quickly negotiate based on reason, striving to restore the original state and expedite commerce."

"A copy of the Tingzhou Tobacco and Alcohol Tax Collection Bureau's tax increase announcement and a guarantee bond form have been sent to the association. Based on this, the regulations regarding the special tax on native tobacco stipulate separate calculations of the quantity of native tobacco leaves that have not had their veins removed and net tobacco leaves that have had their veins removed, with different collection provisions. The original principle was to apply it to the taxation of tobacco leaves. As for the method of including non-special zones into special zones, those taxing tobacco threads are all taxed according to the weight of the tobacco threads at the prescribed rate, regardless of the tobacco leaves required to make the tobacco threads and the amount of veins removed. For the past three years, skin threads, Chaozhou tobacco, etc., have all been taxed according to this method. Therefore, the quantity stipulated for the taxation of skin thread tobacco is 67 catties per hundred packages. The so-called 67 catties refers to the quantity of net tobacco threads, not the quantity of tobacco leaves, and especially disregarding the amount of veins removed."

"The Tingzhou Tobacco and Alcohol Tax Bureau is completely ignorant of the process of handling this case and the original intention of taxing tobacco threads, and has presumptuously acted clever, distorted the established regulations, and falsely associated them with provincial orders (provincial orders for tax increases refer to tobacco, not tobacco threads). They have added tobacco veins to the tobacco threads for joint taxation, treating tobacco leaves and tobacco threads as one, thinking that they can increase the country's tax revenue and perform a small service. However, they are unaware that they are deeply involved in overturning the established deployment. One discrepancy is that even if tobacco threads are taxed, their quantity should not be estimated based on tobacco leaves, but on the amount of veins removed from the tobacco leaves used to make the tobacco threads, which should not be added to the tax outside the quantity of tobacco threads. Tobacco threads and tobacco leaves are different. Tobacco leaves become pure net tobacco leaves on the tax list after the veins are removed. In addition to net tobacco leaves as the main material, tobacco threads also have a large number of ingredients mixed in, such as oil and water, each accounting for 15% to 20%, and color powder, flower petals, etc., accounting for about 5% to over 10%. The quantity of these ingredients is sufficient to offset the quantity of tobacco veins with a surplus. Since these ingredients are not taxable items and have not been marked out as tax-free within the quantity of tobacco threads, how can the tobacco veins be added to the quantity of tobacco threads for joint taxation? The principle is very clear, but if the Tingzhou Tobacco and Alcohol Tax Bureau does not understand, is it because they are harming merchants or is there another purpose? This is the second discrepancy."

"The Ministry of Finance stipulates that the standard for the taxation quantity of skin thread tobacco is originally 67 catties per hundred packages. Later, for the sake of calculation, the Tingzhou Bureau changed it to 70 catties, exceeding the Ministry's stipulation by 3 catties. The merchants did not haggle over such a small amount, which shows that the merchants have done their best to fulfill their tax obligations within their capabilities. Now, due to the addition of tobacco veins to the tax, it has further increased to 91 catties, and they still think it is not enough, ordering tobacco merchants to guarantee that if it exceeds 91 catties, they will be responsible for any tax losses. Such relentless demands are not the original intention of the country to collect taxes. This is the third discrepancy."

"Regarding the inappropriate methods and the tax increases that change established cases, without the approval of superiors, they have prematurely announced and implemented them, which shows their stubbornness. Moreover, they are coercively obtaining guarantee bonds. Merchants do not owe taxes, and they are coerced into adding taxes. Why should they provide guarantees? If it is said that the assumed tax increase method cannot be implemented effectively, so tobacco merchants must provide guarantees to be responsible for supplementary tax payments, then if the superiors reject the bureau's tax increase, who will guarantee and return the tax payments that have already been collected? There is nothing more deceitful than this. In short, methods that are not practical should not be imposed on the people. This is the fourth discrepancy."

"We believe that maintaining national taxes depends on the cooperation of officials and civilians. Unilateral harassment is not appropriate. The quantity of ingredients used in the manufacture of tobacco threads stated by our association is all based on factual circumstances and does not contain any fabrication. There are many tobacco thread factories in Beijing and Shanghai, which can be easily investigated. If your office believes that the investigation is not credible, then for the sake of the merchants expressing their intentions, they can only request that your office change to taxing tobacco leaves. Furthermore, Yongding in Fujian Province has already been designated as a special tax area and should originally tax tobacco leaves instead of tobacco threads. In the past, it was temporarily handled due to the unrest in the area and the changes of the puppet government, and the special tax on tobacco leaves could not be implemented. The reason why the taxation of tobacco threads has not been changed is simply because the method is simple and definite, officials do not create extraneous branches, and the people are content to comply. Now, the Tingzhou Tax Collection Bureau is wantonly creating chaos, destroying established cases, and once the chaos begins, it is difficult to predict the consequences. If there is no proper way to maintain the situation, then following the Ministry's regulations to tax leaves can fundamentally solve the problem."

"As for the Tingzhou Bureau's false accusation that tobacco veins are evading taxes, hoping to supplement them to gain merit, their wishful thinking and erroneous actions have harmed merchants and disregarded regulations. Whether they should be thoroughly dismissed to suit the merchants' situation and protect the credibility of all Ministry regulations is up to your office to weigh. Our association does not dare to request presumptuously. However, the tobacco threads waiting to be transported in Yongding have been obstructed and delayed by the Tingzhou Bureau and cannot be exported. They have been accumulating for a long time, and mold is a concern. Commerce is not smooth, and both domestic and foreign businesses are deeply harmed. As a last resort, we have specially attached a copy of the Tingzhou Bureau's tax increase announcement and a guarantee bond form and submit this document to your office for review. We humbly request that you quickly order the Tingzhou Tobacco and Alcohol Tax Collection Bureau to immediately cancel the tax increase, restore the original state, and expedite the release of tobacco threads waiting for export to relieve tobacco merchants from their predicament. We are extremely anxious and await your orders." Sincerely submitted.

Shen Xiangrui, the director of the Municipal Zoo, went to Japan last October to study and investigate methods of preventing and controlling animal diseases. It was loaded in a wooden cage and unloaded from the ship that evening and transported to the zoo on Wenmiao Road. It will be open to the public for viewing in the next few days.

After questioning, Judge Liu adjourned the hearing for a later date. Zhang Fang was allowed to be released on bail, and Zhang Lou was detained. At about 10:00 am, Prosecutor Tang of the First Court came to the mortuary to conduct an autopsy. One Collision Causes Harm to Three Ships: Lushan Collides with Haiyun, Damages Nanyang, Songshan, and a Barge, Resulting in Significant Losses – Incident Occurs in Front of Yangjiadu 137

The Haiyun, a ship belonging to the state-owned China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, arriving in Shanghai from Lianyungang, was struck by the Lushan, a ship belonging to the Nisshin Kisen Kaisha company, upon reaching the dock. The impact also affected the Nanyang and Songshan vessels, and a barge was crushed, resulting in substantial damage. This newspaper's reporter, upon learning of the incident, went to investigate the situation and will present the details below:

Haiyun Turns Around: The Haiyun, formerly the French ship "D'Artagnan" purchased by the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, is dedicated to transporting freight from the Longhai Railway to the port of Lianyungang. This time, the Haiyun arrived in Shanghai on the morning of the 20th (the day before yesterday), at approximately 10:00 AM. The Haiyun entered Wusong, heading for the Yangjiadu pier in Pudong to unload cargo. The Yangjiadu pier is connected to the Nisshin pier in Pudong. When the Haiyun vessel reached Yangjiadu, it usually turned around before docking. At that time, the river surface was turbulent with strong winds and tides. Captain Huang Hongqian turned the ship around on the river surface. Normally, the ship channel faces towards Pudong when turning. However, the Nisshin Kisen Kaisha's Lushan vessel,

Disregards the River Surface: Ignoring that a ship was turning around on the river, it undocked from the Nisshin pier. It was heading to Fuzhou and Guangdong. When the Lushan left the dock, the stern was facing out from the dock, backing out onto the river surface before heading off. As the stern of the Lushan extended out, the Haiyun was in the process of turning around. Seeing this situation, Captain Huang was alarmed, fearing a major disaster. He quickly changed the Haiyun's ship channel to turn west, hoping to avoid a severe collision. Unfortunately, the Japanese vessel did not stop at this time, possibly because it was too late. As a result, the stern of the Lushan collided with the port side of the Haiyun,

Mid-cabin Collision: Causing damage to the iron plates of the Haiyun's port side mid-cabin. The stern of the Lushan also suffered significant damage due to the excessive recoil. At this point, the hull of the Lushan had not fully left the dock. In front of this vessel were the Songshan and Nanyang vessels. The rear of the Lushan struck the Nanyang. The impact broke the mooring cables, causing the Nanyang to also experience extreme turbulence. It first violently struck a barge that was outside the hull,

Crushed Under the Hull: Causing significant damage. Another barge that was also next to the hull was also damaged. The Songshan vessel was moored at the bow and stern of the Nanyang vessel. It had already loaded its cargo and was carrying passengers, ready to sail to various ports in Northern China. Unexpectedly, after being struck by the Nanyang, the iron anchor of its bow went towards the rear of the Songshan,

Nanyang Breaks Through: Fortunately, the damaged area and the damage to the rear of the Lushan were both above the cargo line, and did not significantly affect navigation. However, both vessels were eager to depart, so they could not stay in Shanghai for long. At the time, the captain reported the incident to Nisshin Kisen Kaisha. Captain Huang Hongqian of the Haiyun also reported the incident to the General Bureau. Nisshin Kisen Kaisha, upon receiving the report, immediately requested that impartial personnel inspect the damage to both vessels, estimate all losses, and prepare to negotiate with the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company. They also instructed the Lushan and Songshan to depart after inspection, with the damaged areas temporarily repaired. Major repairs would be done upon their return to Shanghai. The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company also sent Engineer Zhang to

Inspect the Haiyun: And inquire about the cause of the collision. Engineer Zhang also inspected the situation on both Japanese vessels. The responsibility for this collision lies entirely with the Japanese vessel Lushan, for not considering the presence of a ship in the Huangpu River when setting sail, resulting in this disaster. The Haiyun is not at fault. Yesterday afternoon, the incident was reported to the Navigation Administration Bureau and the insurance company was notified. The insurance company will send personnel to reinspect the case. The issue of responsibility will be negotiated by both parties. The Haiyun suffered minor damage and can still sail to Haizhou Lianyungang this morning. As for the damaged barge, Nisshin will handle the matter. This collision, which damaged two vessels and destroyed a barge, resulted in very significant losses.

Wheeler Speaks on Slaughterhouses: Lecture Given Yesterday at the Lester Institute of Technology 138

The Chinese Institute of Engineers held a meeting yesterday at the Lester Institute of Technology, where Wheeler, a technician from the Public Works Department of the Shanghai Municipal Council, gave a lecture on the Council's plans and equipment for establishing slaughterhouses. He stated that the design of modern slaughterhouses requires careful consideration. For example, when the Municipal Council established a slaughterhouse in this city, it sought the opinions of various experts in order to achieve perfection and provide the residents of this city with a modern, scientific slaughterhouse that could provide ample meat. The establishment of slaughterhouses is entirely due to the large urban population and the demand for high-quality meat products, rather than the meaning of slaughtering animals in a humane manner. After the establishment of slaughterhouses, the benefits include lower meat prices, concentrated livestock, convenient veterinary inspections, the ability to improve breeding through the study of animal diseases, and the promotion of legislation to protect public health. Dead animals can be disinfected and sold for other uses, avoiding waste. In some countries, hygiene is not considered when raising livestock, and the quality of meat is not considered. These types of livestock only have the opportunity to be inspected after being transported to slaughterhouses. Purchasers can see whether there is a slaughterhouse inspection stamp and know what to choose. During the lecture, a video on the equipment and slaughtering process of slaughterhouses was shown, providing a reference for engineering professionals. Members of the association are scheduled to visit the Municipal Council's slaughterhouse on Saturday.

The Continental Industrial Company has been operating in the Huai salt industry for many years, with branches in Haizhou, Bengbu, Nanjing, Jiujiang, Hankou, Yichang, and Shashi. Robbery of Guns from Zhabei Corps Police: Four Robbers Caught in Tea House, Two Fled Under Cover of Darkness 142

Yesterday afternoon, the Bazizhao Police Station of the North Station Branch received a tip that the robbers involved in the recent robberies of guns from the Pengpu District Defense Corps and the police officers on Zhongxing Road near the Bazizhao Police Station were meeting on the upper floor of the Sande Tea House at 330 Zhongshan Road, planning further criminal activities. Upon receiving the information, the police station immediately dispatched Inspector Li Jinrong, Sergeant Chuan Yongkang, police officers Han Pingzhou and Qi Wenbin, and more than ten detectives to secretly surround the location. After being identified by an informant, the police detectives issued an order and apprehended the four robbers who were drinking tea. A 4-inch pistol and four bullets were found on one of the robbers. Unexpectedly, two other robbers sitting at a nearby table fled downstairs upon seeing their accomplices being captured. The police detectives noticed this and immediately went downstairs in pursuit. The two robbers desperately fled into the wilderness to hide. Seeing that the police detectives were closing in, they opened fire to resist arrest while running. Gunshots were heard continuously. However, due to the darkness and the wilderness, the two robbers managed to escape. Afterwards, the area was searched, and another 4-inch pistol and two bullets abandoned by the robbers were found. The four captured robbers were taken back to the police station. After interrogation, they identified themselves as Dong Jingzhai, 30 years old, Xiao Fulong, 28 years old, and Qi Defu, 34 years old, all from Jinan, and Wang Huanting, from Fengtian, 33 years old. The pistol and bullets were found on Xiao Fulong, who claimed that the weapons were supplied by someone else. They confessed to the numerous gun robbery cases. When asked about the names of the masterminds, they claimed that one was Li Shouheng from Jinan, residing at 3 Zhonghua Fang, Zhonghua New Road, and the other was Zhao Debiao from Tancheng, 27 years old, residing at 6 Xiangshan Lane, Yanjiage Road. All the weapons and criminal plans were directed by these two individuals. The two who resisted arrest in the wilderness were also these two, they said. After receiving the confession, the police station immediately dispatched detectives to secretly arrest them. However, Li Shouheng had already fled. It was not until approximately 10:30 PM that Zhao Debiao and his mistress, Bu Sanyuan, a local resident aged 29, were captured in Xiangshan Lane. After being taken to the police station for interrogation, Zhao claimed to be working as a gatekeeper at Tianyun Paradise, and remained evasive. Bu Sanyuan claimed that she had only recently become acquainted with Zhao. She worked as a female tea server in the Shenqu theater at the Paradise and did not know much about Zhao's activities. The police station then handed over the captured criminals, along with the guns and bullets, to the General Bureau for further investigation. In the meantime, they continued to dispatch detectives to pursue Li Shouheng and bring him to justice. At the same time, a man from Jiangbei named Wang Yongfu, 25 years old, was struck by five bullets while the robbers were being arrested and fell in the wilderness. He was subsequently found by the police officers, who took him to the hospital for treatment. He suffered one gunshot wound to the neck and four to his legs. The injured man claimed to be a tailor and was unable to avoid the gunfire. However, according to the police station's investigation, the man was injured in the wilderness. At the time of the shootout between the police and the robbers, there were no other people walking around, so it is difficult to immediately determine whether he was a robber or a civilian. A fortune teller has been consulted.

Shooting Case on Route Doumer: Shanghai Police Arrest Two Key Suspects 143

—Various Parties Maintain Strict Secrecy and Refuse to Announce Details—

An Outer News Agency reported in the Continental Daily that two Chinese men, said to be directly related to the shooting of Japanese sailor Nakayama Hideo on Route Doumer on November 9th last year, were brought to the First Special District Court yesterday for a brief hearing. They were then returned to the Central Police Station for custody under strict guard.

The interrogation was conducted in extreme secrecy. The only attendees were a small number of police officers directly involved in the case. A reporter from the Continental Daily witnessed the two suspects being taken to the court, but despite his best efforts to inquire about the details of the case, he was unable to obtain any information. According to reports, the Legal Department of the Shanghai Municipal Council informed reporters that they had received instructions not to disclose any information about the case. However, it has now been confirmed that the two men were arrested in connection with the Nakayama Hideo shooting case and are believed to be directly involved in the shooting.

According to a reliable source, one of the two men was arrested in Tianjin last week and was immediately extradited to Shanghai. The other was arrested yesterday morning by the detectives of the Route des Soeurs Police Station.

Japanese officials are also maintaining the same secrecy regarding the matter. However, given that the arrest of the two men has already been made, it seems undeniable. It is said that the two men were taken to the Central Police Station yesterday morning for temporary detention, and then taken to the court for interrogation in the afternoon.

What is strange is that most of the personnel at the Central Police Station are unaware of this matter. Those who know about it are also maintaining secrecy and refuse to disclose any information.

The case of the shooting of Japanese sailor Nakayama Hideo occurred on November 9th last year. The authorities offered a reward of 1,000 yuan for the capture of the murderer.

Zhong Yuliang Requests Correction of Unauthorized Excavation of Abandoned Graves 146

The practice of grave robbing has been prevalent in the four rural areas of this city, especially in Gaoqiao in Pudong. Now, former Municipal Councilor Zhong Yuliang of the district has submitted a case to the Farmers' Association. The case proposes that Yin [surname only] is encroaching on the official river and instructing the excavation of abandoned graves, requesting that the situation be corrected. The Qingpu River is a major river in our rural area. Due to the large scale of the project, it has been silted up for decades and impossible to dredge. In the past, the joint efforts of the three counties of Baoshan and Chuansha were required to dredge it. All of us villagers should cherish it and avoid clogging it up. However, Yin has privately filled in the Qingpu River behind his residence, encroaching on more than two zhang (during the river dredging, large trees were used as boundaries, and the current trees are over two zhang from [what is considered the original location], and there is a public land of one zhang to the west of the trees, which can be proven by the Qing Dynasty survey map). Yin also slightly expanded on the east bank, hoping to deceive the public. As a result, the straight river has become a back-bow shape. The surrounding area is silted up, making it difficult for boats to travel and water to flow smoothly, harming merchants, travelers, and farmers. There have been consecutive years of crop failure, with far-reaching impacts. In addition, there is a grave robbing problem in our hometown. When Yuliang was a Municipal Councilor, he submitted a request to the Shanghai Municipal Government for a public ban, which was approved. Now, Yin is instructing the excavation of ownerless graves in order to buy grave bricks and stones for building family shrines and viewing platforms. The foundations of the platforms were originally abandoned graves, which have now been almost completely occupied and excavated. More than ten other abandoned graves have been destroyed in the four rural areas, and the buying continues. As a result, even graves with owners have been excavated. Encroaching on the official river and instructing the excavation of abandoned graves both involve violating the law. Yuliang has repeatedly advised Yin in person, but to no avail. He sent a letter of sincere advice, which was also ignored. The Qingpu River is related to the water conservancy of the entire township, and grave robbing is related to customs and traditions. Therefore, I dare to recount the circumstances and request that your association correct the situation, order Yin to restore the Qingpu River to its original state, order him to stop buying abandoned grave bricks and stones, and demolish the foundations of the occupied abandoned graves, so as to set an example for others. Whether this is appropriate, please make a public decision. Respectfully submitted by proponent Zhong Yuliang.

Details of the Sudden Death of the Giant Elephant in the Municipal Zoo – Colleagues in the Zoo Express Deep Sorrow 150

The news of the sudden death of a giant elephant in the Municipal Zoo on Wenmiao Road due to electric shock has been briefly reported. However, the cause of death is not clear. The Datong News Agency reporter learned from the zoo that the gray elephant was purchased in the 23rd year of the Republic of China and transported to Shanghai in July of that year. It was put on display in the park at a cost of 2,800 yuan. The zoo immediately purchased the base in the southwest corner of the park adjacent to the park and built an elephant house, intending to ensure the safety of the giant elephant's life. Because elephants like heat and have a huge body, the materials of the elephant house are all made of steel and cement. There is an open space in front of the house, a swimming pool, and two wall-mounted stoves in the house. The cleanliness and health of the elephant are fully considered. Recently, spherical parasites were found on the skin of the elephant. After rigorous treatment, it has not yet recovered. Suddenly, on the 19th of the month, it jumped violently in the middle of the night, destroyed the door lock, and died of electric shock. The colleagues in the park usually work carefully, but unexpectedly the elephant died suddenly and unexpectedly. They were unable to rescue it and were all extremely sad.

(A) The total amount of exchange notes issued is 25,853,171 yuan in silver, including 23,368,0182 yuan in silver notes and 2,485,0889 yuan in fractional currency notes. The total amount of exchange note reserve is 25,853,171 yuan, including 17,768,0371 yuan in cash reserve. This cash reserve includes 14,556,4843.7 yuan stored in the general and branch treasuries of the three banks' issuing branches, and 3,211,9527.29 yuan stored in the same industry. The guaranteed reserve is equivalent to 8,085,0700 yuan in silver. (B) The total amount of exchange notes issued is 373,324.7 yuan, and the total amount of gold exchange note reserve is 373,324.7 yuan. This reserve includes 7,351.95 taels of standard gold, which is equivalent to 373,324.7 yuan in customs gold at the fixed price of 5.0779. According to Article 22 of the Central Bank Law, the cash reserve should be at least 60%, and the rest should be guaranteed reserves in the form of legal guarantees. The results of this inspection show that the cash reserve exceeds 60%, and the guaranteed reserve is within 40%, which is in accordance with the law. This is a special report. April 20, 1936, Chairman of the Board of Supervisors of the Central Bank, Li Fuxun, Supervisors Xie Mengjun, Bei Songsun, Qin Runqing, Yu Qiaqing, Lin Kanghou, and Xu Ji.

The Insurance Industry in Shanghai 160

— Chief Editor of China WeChat

(General Conditions of Industry and Commerce in Shanghai, No. 23)

1. The Evolution of the Insurance Industry in Shanghai

The pioneers of the insurance industry in Shanghai were undoubtedly the British firms, Yongfu and Small Eastern. These two companies were established in 1836. At that time, their scale was very small, and the Chinese people did not understand the nature and significance of insurance. Therefore, most of the insured were foreigners. In 1885, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company established the Renjihe Insurance Company, which marked the beginning of our country's engagement in fire and marine insurance. From 1888 to 1900, Yongfu Company compiled a Chinese mortality experience table and began to underwrite Chinese life insurance. Subsequently, American companies such as New York Life Insurance Co. and The Equitable Life Ins. Co. of New York established branches in China. In 1899, the China Yongnian Life Insurance Company was established, marking the beginning of Chinese involvement in life insurance. Thereafter, the number of foreign fire and marine insurance branches established in Shanghai was innumerable. After 1905, Chinese insurance companies began to flourish, including companies such as Hezong, Huaan, Huaxing, Huacheng, Wanfeng, and Fuan. In 1905, the Shanghai Insurance Association was established. At this time, Chinese insurance companies had gradually grown in scale. Subsequently, companies such as Huaan Hequn Insurance Company, Yongning Insurance Firm, the Insurance Department of the Central Trust Company, and the Insurance Department of the Ning Shao Merchant Shipping Company were successively established. Xianshi, Yongan and others re-established branches in Shanghai. Thus, the insurance industry in Shanghai became increasingly prosperous. In the past three years, the Shanghai financial sector has been affected by the decline of industry and commerce, the bankruptcy of rural areas, and the concentration of capital in cities. It has also competed to invest its surplus capital in insurance, resulting in significant progress. Not only have new companies (such as Taiping Tianyi, etc.) been established one after another, but the strong capital of Japanese companies, far surpassing others, is also a special phenomenon in today's overall economic downturn.

2. The Current Situation of Insurance in Shanghai

1. A Comparison of the Number of Chinese and Foreign Merchants

Currently, in terms of the number of insurance companies in Shanghai, there are more than 140 foreign companies and only 26 Chinese companies, with two Sino-foreign joint ventures. In terms of capital, the paid-up capital of Chinese companies, including branches, totals more than 25 million yuan. Although 80% of foreign companies are agency-based, their capital figures are difficult to calculate temporarily. However, the capital of the American Insurance Association alone reaches more than 136.4 million US dollars. The meager capital of Chinese merchants is indeed vastly different from that of foreign merchants.

2. An Overview of Insurance Companies from Various Countries in Shanghai

Among the foreign insurance companies in Shanghai, the British have the largest influence, followed by the Americans. There are very few French and Japanese insurance companies. The influence of German, Italian, Swiss, Austrian, and other nationalities is even weaker. A detailed description follows:

A. British Merchants: Among British insurance companies, Union Insurance Society of Canton Ltd, Employes' Liability Assurance Corp, Ltd, South British Insurance Co, and Sun Insurance Office, Ltd are the leaders. The contents of the first two companies are briefly described below:

1. Union Insurance Society of Canton Ltd. The company was founded in 1835 and registered with the Hong Kong government. Its total capital is one million pounds, and its paid-up capital is 540,000 pounds. The head office is located in Hong Kong, and branches are located in Guangzhou, Hankou, Beiping, Tianjin, Shanghai, etc. It specializes in marine, fire, automobile, and credit insurance, and is a joint-stock company. Its directors are C. G. Mackie, S.H. Dodwell, J. Owen Hughes, G, Miskino, T.A. Mitcbell, K.S. Monison. The general manager is A. W. Hughes. The Shanghai branch is located at No. 6 Bund and was established in 1908. The current manager is G. G. Franklin.

2. Employers’ Liability Assurance Corporation, Ltd. The company's head office is located in London. The Shanghai branch was established in 1880 in the Sassoon Building on the Bund. The manager is Mr. Bang T.R., who is currently the chairman of the Shanghai Foreign Merchants Fire Insurance Association. The company's total assets are 17 million pounds, and its annual premium income is more than 7 million pounds.

B. American Merchants: Among American insurance companies, American Foreign Insurance Association, Insurance Company of North America, and AmericaAsiatic Unjerwrite, Fed, Inc, U.S.A have the largest scope. A detailed description of their contents follows:

1. American Foreign Insurance Association. The head office is located at 80 Maiden Lane, New York, USA. The Shanghai branch is located at 51 Guangdong Road. It is jointly organized by the following seventeen American companies: American Insurance Co. New York N.J, Continental Insurance Co, New York, Fidelity-Phenix Fire Ins. Co. New York Fire Association Philadelphia, Pa, Glens, Fa;cs Ins Bo. New York. Great American Ins.Co, New York, Halifax Fire Ins. Co, conneticut Home Indemnity Co, New York, Natonal Fire Ins Co. Hartford Conn, NEw HaCi. hire Fire Ins. Co, Springield Frei &nMisrae In . Co. Minnesota, United States Fie Ins.Co,New York, Westchester Fire In s. Co, New York,& Home Ins,Co, NewYork, U.S.A

The above seventeen companies have a total paid-up capital of US$136,442,737.00, a public reserve of US$381,119,074.00, and total assets worth US$707,939,324.00 in 1932. The premium income for that year reached US$247,391,945.00. The association underwrites insurance of various natures. Its annual premium income in China is one million Chinese currency. The chief representative in China is M, and the Shanghai assistant manager is Mr. Muldoon A.G. Branches are also located in Hankou and Tianjin.

2. Insurance Company of North America. The company was established in 1792. The head office is in Philadelphia, USA. Branches in China are located in Hong Kong, Shanghai, Tianjin, etc. The Shanghai branch is located at No. 12 Jiujiang Road. Its paid-up capital is US$12 million, and its current assets are worth more than US$72 million. It underwrites insurance of various natures. Its general manager is Kreulen R.A., the manager of the Shanghai branch is Petersen V.I.G, and the Chinese manager is Mr. Zhu Yanbin.

3. American Asiatic Underwriters, Fed, Inc, U.S.A. The company is an agency-based company, established in the 9th year of the Republic of China. The head office of Liaodong is located at No. 17 Bund in this city. Branches are located in Hankou, Tianjin, Chongqing, Guangzhou, Hangzhou, Fuzhou, Hong Kong, Yangon, Little Luzon, Batavia, Haiphong, New York, etc. Its paid-up capital is 2,797,202.80 yuan, and its public reserve and reserve fund are 1,074,764.89 yuan (as of 1933). The chairman and general manager is Slan C.V, who is currently the chairman of American Asiatic Bank and a director of Sihai Taishan and other insurance companies. It underwrites various types of insurance and acts as an agent for as many as 26 insurance companies. Its annual premium income reaches 3 million yuan, but it decreased to more than 810,000 yuan in the previous year. Its profits over the years are as follows: 252,33.04 taels in the 19th year of the Republic of China, 302,043.62 taels in the 20th year of the Republic of China, 78,657.85 taels in the 12th year of the Republic of China, 344,808.77 yuan in the 22nd year of the Republic of China, and 144,199.65 yuan in the 23rd year of the Republic of China.

In terms of investment, the company holds shares in American Asiatic Life Insurance Company, accounting for 25,000 shares out of its total of 40,000 shares. It invests in French American Insurance Company, accounting for half of its assets. In addition, it is a shareholder of Sihai Insurance Company. It can be called a giant among insurance agencies in Shanghai. However, since the liquidation of American Asiatic Bank, the company's investment of 183,000 yuan in the bank has been lost, and its financial strength has inevitably been slightly affected. Shen Bao National Products Special Issue

National Products Market in the Capital 161

— Shouqiu

In the past two or three years, the voice of advocating national products in the capital has indeed been very high, and some people also know the importance of advocating national products. Under such circumstances, national products markets have emerged accordingly. There are a total of four national products markets in the current capital. The oldest one is the national products market in the Huaiqing Bridge National Products Exhibition Hall. The largest one is the recently opened Central Market. The situation of these four national products markets is described separately below:

Central Market The Central Market has only been open for two or three months. It is located on Zhongzheng Road, not far from Xinjiekou Square, and is also very close to Taiping Road, Zhongshan Road, and others, so the location is very good. The shops inside are also very complete, and there is also a Bank of China and a Central Garden, which other markets do not have. There is a Chinese restaurant upstairs: There is also a Western restaurant: There is also a barber shop. There are more than one hundred shops in the whole market. There is a United Sales Office of Shanghai National Products Factories, which are all famous factories in Shanghai, and it is the most exciting and valuable market in the whole market. The office is on the third floor. Slogans advocating national products and new life are hung on the walls and pillars in the market. Salespersons also have a badge for easy identification. Therefore, the order is indeed very orderly. To the right of the market is a Dahua Cinema, but it has not yet opened. If it opens, the business of the market will definitely be much better than it is now.

A special feature of this market is that the change is not based on the market rate of silver coins in Nanjing, but on the legal price stipulated by the Ministry of Finance. Because the market rate in Nanjing is that one yuan of legal tender can be exchanged for three thousand one hundred and several dozen copper coins, while in this market, it is calculated at three thousand coins per yuan, regardless of change in or out.

National Products Market The National Products Market of Huaiqing Bridge is affiliated with the National Products Exhibition Hall of the Ministry of Industry. It has been around for about ten years in Nanjing! However, because the location is not very suitable, it seems to be at a disadvantage in terms of competition. However, a road has now been built there, and transportation is still considered convenient. In addition, the market can be pragmatic in all business operations, which is very commendable. The gate of the market is on the left side of the National Products Exhibition Hall. Probably two months ago? The market has been transferred to the management of the Nanjing Municipal Government and is no longer related to the Ministry of Industry.

China National Products Company Its address is next to the Central Bank on Qi Wang Street, Jiankang Road, which is also a lively location. It has been open for one year and six months, and the business is said to be very developed. Because it is run by the Nanjing Municipal Government, it naturally has some advantages in almost every aspect, but the location of the company is very small, which seems to be a fly in the ointment. However, it is indeed not easy to find a building with a large area on that road. Fortunately, the company's business will not be diminished by the small location!

Because the company is run by the municipal government, the quality of the goods is very good, and the price is fair, which is commendable.

Great China Market It seems that it has not been open for a year. Its address is the old site of the World Hotel on Taiping Road Men Zhai Bridge. In addition to the main entrance, a door is also opened in the north. Speaking of Taiping Road, it is also a lively road in Nanjing, but for some reason, the business of the market is not very good. Recently, the market held a big sale for a month, and those who bought one yuan or more were given a scholarship lottery ticket. At the same time, there were also loss leaders. Invincible Tooth Powder, three bags can be bought for one cent; Guben Soap, one piece is sold for one dime, and Double Coin brand rubber shoes are also sold for fifty-five cents, which can be said to be a truly big sacrifice! But except for the loss leaders that were bought by many people, the rest of the business is still very sluggish.

In addition to the four mentioned above, there is no fifth national products market in Nanjing at present. Finally, what I want to report is that the Central Market will organize an evaluation committee to prevent raising prices. Perhaps the market has heard the rumors outside! Because many people say that the prices of goods in the market are relatively expensive.
