Two Lines of Progress for National Products 164

— Xuan Wan

At the current stage, there are two very clear and correct lines of progress for national products industry unfolding before us. One is to actively seek the development of overseas markets, especially to expand trade in various places in Nanyang, so as to eliminate the trade deficit and increase exports. The other is to strive to make domestic products penetrate deeply into the people, and try to promote sales to various provinces in the border areas, and form a national production and sales cooperation network.

In recent years, the future of our national products has been due to the hard work of the national products industry, the protection of the government, and the enthusiastic support of the entire people, which has indeed enabled the industrial sector—especially the general mechanical industry manufacturers—to lay a very solid foundation. The future work should be to earnestly develop production, expand sales, and awaken all people, so that any people in urban and rural areas and overseas Chinese have places to identify and purchase national products. Naturally, we should step up our work, work hard, and urgently need our industrial sector to determine a concrete plan to gradually make it actively realized.

Regarding these two lines of progress, the recent trends in the development of national products, it is worth mentioning here that in terms of promoting sales in border areas, Mr. Ma Hongkui, Chairman of Ningxia Province, came to Shanghai last week to contact national products manufacturers to hold a national products exhibition there, so that national products will progress to the northwest—after Xi'an and Lanzhou, now to Ningxia, the farthest frontier. In terms of developing overseas markets, it was recently heard that the China National Foreign Trade Association is actively preparing to organize overseas sales teams, training personnel, and studying various steps to implement new plans to first go to Nanyang for exhibitions and develop overseas markets.

History teaches us: "Empty words are useless, and things are important to practice." We are now only from the two lines of progress of national products—striving to develop overseas markets and promoting sales in border areas—that everyone unites and cooperates, and moves forward very bravely.

Spring and Autumn

Anecdotes 167

— (Xiaoting)

In our daily diet, after eating vegetables for too long, we feel that the taste of meat is rich and beautiful. After eating fish and meat, we feel bored, and we feel that vegetables are fresh and tender. In life adjustment, all things should be viewed in this way.

Bridges are easy to fall from when they are high, and roads are difficult to run when they are far. Those in the mountains do not know the height of the mountains, and those on the peaks do not know the danger of the peaks. Breaking through difficulties and advancing bravely, the Himalayas are high, but they cannot hinder the feet of explorers.

Modern people do things like old women reading scriptures, only seeking to read them fluently, not seeking their meaning. Giving weight to quantity and not quality is a common problem of modern human beings.

When young people study, it is better to study how to use living words than to turn over dead dictionaries, and it is better to read ancient and modern books than to write articles indiscriminately.

Random Talk on Science 168

— Zhou Xian

Modern new inventions in science are one after another for us to enjoy. What a happy thing this is? But when we sit back and enjoy these scientific inventions, how should we commemorate the scientists who invented these things?

Every scientist who invents something is definitely not just a matter of one stroke of the hand to succeed. History tells us that some scientists have spent years or decades, or even their entire lives, in test tubes, microscopes, or other scientific instruments. Moreover, there are also some who have studied for a lifetime and have not succeeded, and leave the unfinished work to the deceased, or to the scientists of the next generation to study and invent. This kind of research spirit seems to be somewhat foolish, because for the sake of spending a lifetime of energy, even if there is an invention, but by the time of the invention, oneself is already gray-haired and dim-sighted, and in reality, one can no longer enjoy it. To make oneself suffer and create others, wouldn't that be the number one fool in the world? But scientists don't think so. They only know that there is science, and they are willing to coexist and die with science, and finally evolve our world to today's material civilization.

For example, without using a fire drill, we can use matches to make fire. Without lighting a fire, we can use electric lights to get light. How convenient is this? With a seemingly very simple radio, you can receive sounds broadcast from every corner of the earth from the air. It seems that all sounds are emitted in the small room. How magical is that? It is said that in recent years, wireless telegraphy has also achieved considerable success, which is even more mysterious. We can only marvel at the greatness of science. To say it again, Wanshan Wanli can shorten the journey with trains and cars. The vast ocean can be reached on time by giant ships that ride the wind and waves. That's already quite something. Now, the rising star of airplanes, like flying birds, can reach everywhere, and the journey of thousands of miles can be reached in the morning and evening. Great science, it's really amazing.

But in these years, although science is so developed, there are still many things in front of us, waiting for humans to invent. Such as the prevention of natural disasters, the treatment of diseases, and even interplanetary traffic, etc., in the next few centuries, scientists who benefit humankind are needed for their efforts. Naturally, our descendants may be several times happier than us in terms of the material enjoyment of science.

"Talent Accepted" 169

— Li Guang

A few days ago, I happened to read Mr. Taofen's "Recollections of Drifting Footprints," in which there was a passage that said:

Once, an American middle-aged woman brought her young daughter to travel to England. Introduced by a friend, she rented a room from the family I was staying with, saying she would stay for a week. After she and her daughter moved in, I was busy with work, leaving early and returning late, so I hadn't met them. That evening, the landlady casually talked to her about me, praising me profusely. When the American woman heard that there was a "Chinaman" living in the house, even though she had never met or spoken to me, she resolutely said to the landlady, "I can't live in the same house as a 'Chinaman'!" The next morning, she hurriedly moved out. The landlady was secretly surprised, wondering why "Chinaman" made people avoid him like a venomous snake, causing people to hate him so much!

It is no secret that Westerners look down on us descendants of the Yellow Emperor. But it is not as extreme as the American woman's contempt and disgust. Perhaps Mr. Taofen intended to inspire the awakening of the Chinese people, and I dare not fully believe that such a thing actually happened.

One day, I was walking alone in the park and caught sight of an amah leading a little Western child, sitting on a recliner under a shady tree to rest. Suddenly, a woman with a yellow face also brought a child (but this child was not Western) and walked to the tree, sitting on the other end of the recliner. The little Western child immediately pulled a face, opened his small mouth, and said in a scolding tone: "Get away! You can't sit here with me!" The amah then acted as a translator for her young master, saying to the woman: "He doesn't like you sitting here with him, please go away!" The woman had no choice but to walk away resentfully.

At that time, when I saw this situation, I was saddened for a long time. How could a mere child be so arrogant? This is enough to confirm the complete truth of Mr. Taofen's words.

Phoenix Replacing the Nest 170

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter 1: Sipping Tea and Engaging in Idle Chat by a Night Window Listening to the Rain, Startled by Beauty in a Flower-Filled Lane

Twenty years ago, the revolutionary army had just stabilized Jiangnan. The national calendar had not yet been adopted by society. The people still followed the customs that had been passed down for thousands of years, celebrating the old lunar year. Although Nanjing was a large city in Jiangnan, its people were no less conservative than those in any inland city. Around the Lantern Festival in the first month, bright red "Welcoming Spring" posters still adorned the walls of people's homes. In the rainy and gloomy alleys, the double doors of houses were tightly closed between the walls on either side, with the red spring couplets displayed straightly to passersby, fully expressing the festive atmosphere. The sky was about to darken, and a young man of nearly twenty, wearing a gray cotton robe and a peaked cap, came into the alley, carrying a bag in his left hand and holding a blue cloth umbrella in his right. The sound of his leather shoes walking on the cobblestones on the ground was not very loud, suggesting that he was walking slowly and lightly. He stopped at a black wooden door and knocked on the door knocker a few times. The door opened, and a middle-aged woman came out. When she saw the young man, a smile immediately spread across her worried face. She asked, "You're back very late today, are your studies even busier?" The young man simply called out "Mom" and, while putting away his umbrella, asked, "Isn't Aunt Liu at home? Why did you come to open the door yourself?" The old lady said, "Aunt Liu's contract is up, I let her go back." As she spoke, she closed the door and led her son inside. The structure of houses in cities was generally the same, in a long, linear style. Large houses had one courtyard leading into another, up to six or seven courtyards. Smaller houses had two courtyards, or one and a half. The mother and son lived in the front courtyard, a small three-room space with a brick and stone patio. The patio was not small, with half a flower bed on which grew a clump of nandina and a small tree with a bent trunk. Because it was early spring, it was not yet clear what kind of tree it was. But these two things showed that this family did not have a vulgar air. From the living room on the left, a room led directly to the wing room next to the patio, forming a long study. The young man put his umbrella outside and walked into the room. His mother carried a kerosene lamp and followed him in. The young man exclaimed, took the lamp with both hands, and said with a smile, "Mom, why are you serving me? You shouldn't have dismissed Aunt Liu. She was also very careful in her work." The old lady said, "I didn't dismiss her because she didn't do her job well. I was thinking that if you're not home, and it's just me, I can do all the trivial things myself, so why hire someone? Although the wages saved are limited, a worker's food and drink are considerable each month. Not having this person can save several dollars each month."

Special Feature

Night on Zhu Bao San Road 171

— Chen Liang

Strings of red firecrackers stretched from one house to another. Bars, dance halls, cafes, hotels... these places of intoxication and enjoyment were densely packed along the short Zhu Bao San Road. During the day, it was quiet, like a typhoid patient in a coma, but at night it became restless. Alcohol, tobacco, powder... a mixture of smells, jazz music, hysterical laughter, drunken ramblings... continued until midnight, until dawn...

Foreign sailors wearing white cloth hats, with red, monkey-like faces, stumbled out of the white-painted glass doors, shouting boisterously. A group of rickshaws rushed forward, shouting a few broken phrases in English: "Sir, I pull you to the dock to return to warship." "I pull you to whorehouse!" However, the warrior of the civilized country got angry, raised his fist, and threw it at the rickshaw puller's neck. Then, the line of rickshaws scattered, cursing.

The flower girls crowded in, their hair disheveled, wearing cheap powder, unfashionable cloth cheongsams, mud-stained leather shoes, their dry hands holding a flower, trying to pin it on the sailor's collar, pinning it... entangled. The warrior of the civilized country was not angry, his face flushed with a drunken smile, he took out silver coins from his pocket and threw them into the flower girl's hand, onto the dark cement corner. Then, the flower girl smiled, seeming to celebrate the harvest of profit. But, was this really their harvest? We don't know how much profit was harvested by others. Now, they were throwing down some crumbs, were they smiling? Were they celebrating? The ignorant flower girls would not understand, for them, it was for the sake of maintaining their livelihood. And the rickshaw puller had failed.

The rickshaw pullers knew the fists of the civilized warriors, even the bayonets, their own blood.

And the second batch of foreign sailors stumbled out of the bar, the rickshaw pullers, the flower girls, the Eurasians of about ten years old crowded in. The night on Zhu Bao San Road was lively, until dawn...

Men are More Beautiful than Women 172

— Yi An

Men's appearance is more beautiful than women's, even in Hollywood, which is full of beauties. On the surface, women seem more beautiful, but the fact is not so. The reason women seem beautiful is because of makeup, hairstyle adjustments, and the colors of their clothes. The reason men seem less attractive than women is because their hair is cut uniformly, and they cannot create any hairstyles to adjust their appearance. The clothes they wear are also similar in style. If you dress women the same as men, and cut their hair like men, then they would probably be far less attractive than men. In general, men's eyebrows, eyelashes, and skin tone are better than women's, and this is due to natural talent. In a family with many children, the brothers are always more beautiful than their sisters.

This is the meaning of "nature," not my personal opinion. Men, like other male animals, are shaped to attract the attention of the opposite sex, while women are the ones who choose their mates. But later, because of the evolution of society, men became the masters of society, and they seized the power to choose their mates. As a result, women had to become the ones who attracted the attention of the opposite sex—look at the situation now.

Small Garden

The Purple Bamboo Shoots are Plump as Spring Ends 173

— Shu Fan

Bamboo shoots are bamboo sprouts, tender and pure, with a lasting and clear taste; they are suitable for use in meals at any time of the year. Since ancient times, those who were content with poverty cultivated gardens and vegetable patches, praising vegetable roots as the greatest delicacy; they did not know that the taste of vegetables was light and not substantial, and compared to the sharp tips of the bamboo shoots emerging from the soil, they were ultimately inferior. Now, if we try to compare dishes to people, then scallions and bok choy are like reclusive guests in the mountains and forests, aloof and slightly lacking in depth. Bamboo shoots, on the other hand, are like hermits in the fields, their essence simple and unadorned, yet still retaining a secluded and cool air. As for pork and sashimi, with their round and fishy taste, they are simply like greedy merchants and inferior officials, not worth discussing. I once visited a monastery during the season when flowers were falling, begging for food from the kitchen. The fragrance floated in the air, everything mixed with the yellow tips of bamboo shoots; lingering in the intestines and tongue, I felt that there was no better taste in the world! But the monks still said apologetically: "We have little to offer our guests, please forgive our neglect!" I thought to myself that in the market, one pound cost a thousand coins, regarded as a precious delicacy, and poor families were lucky to taste them, while the monks ate them every day without any appreciation; following this reasoning, monks are always beyond this world, is it merely because the famous mountains are occupied too often? Because of this, I was envious of escaping to Chan Buddhism.

In the past, I stayed in Fuchun as a guest in the house of Lord Mei Fengxiao, drinking three dou of sorghum wine, letting me get drunk and chant. At that time, the reeds on the river were plump, and the forest orchids in the mountains were blooming; the old servant would dig them up with a hoe in the morning dew, picking them daily to serve as side dishes, resembling white snow lotuses. The residents here live by weaving paper, relying on bamboo rather than mulberry trees in their free time among the ten acres of land. Therefore, along the river and slopes, the bamboo grew abundantly in the clear wind, and every spring, they sprouted everywhere; bamboo shoots were to them like betel nuts to Lingnan and water shield to Xianghu, and it was much easier to obtain than fish and shrimp. And I was content with it, forgetting all other tastes. Sometimes I would sit until the spring stars faded, a thin cold mist blurred the lamp, the old servant knew I liked to drink, and would bring out leftover dregs to relieve the chill; my father, fearing the flavor of the wine was lacking, further gathered a few of the tender shoots from the hedge corner, roasting them over pine fire; they were slightly charred and peeled for eating, a sweet fragrance locked in my tongue, surpassing the roasted taro of the ancient temple, or the noisy crowds of the streets; I felt that the flavors of the past were not yet perfect. So I made another vow, when will I be able to build a hut on a bend of the Chunjiang River?

In the spring of Jiaxu, I returned to my hometown for a short rest, enjoying the tranquility of the Xi Stream. One day, from the Zhuxi Lake, I climbed Mount Xulang, and traced the source of the stream to the Qi family. The mountains were like urns, the sunlight all green, countless ancient trees, with bamboo soaring green among them. Leaning on them, I surveyed, and purple buds touched my shoes; there were also a few new bamboo shoots, just shedding their powdery sheaths, unfolding their natural potential; I guessed they grew tall, weaving green past my lap. Thinking of the difficulty of nurturing one thing so much, how could I bear to trample on them even more? So I stood listening to the flow of the spring, the singing of the birds, the harmony of the pine and the wind, entrusting my ears and eyes to them. At noon, I ate my meal, the mountain family lacked fish and meat, and cut off spring wine, so I indulged myself in a steaming bowl of fragrant rice and bamboo shoots, filled to the brim. When hunger struck at sunset, they brought out dried bamboo shoots, extremely sweet and clear, realizing that what I had tasted on the river was not enough. The next morning, before the morning dew had dried, they gathered wild mushrooms in a basket, and stewed them with bamboo shoots; they were sweet and mellow, the color turned like amber, were these the dishes of mountain guests? Or the relics of the upper immortals? The taste of Great Harmony, indescribable, so I longed for mountain living.

My family also had a small garden, and opening the curtain, there was a bamboo fence, luxuriantly growing, where I slept and studied in my childhood. I remember when spring was ending, every time I saw my sister picking bamboo shoots, I had to whisper, "Please leave a little for the next meal!" And so it became routine. There were also those that were fortunate enough to avoid the axe, and I would see them grow from inches to feet, from shoots to leaves, and I would remember them silently. Today, those that just reached the window, I had looked at them overnight, and they were already slightly obstructing the sunlight; before long, they would go over the eaves; and by summer, they could attract a cool wind. Occasionally facing them, I often indulged in foolish thoughts: if I were a bamboo shoot, I would be friends with the cicadas every day. At that time, the clear sounds were still singing, my eyes secretly watching, unable to restrain myself. Since falling into the Jianghu world, this dream has long disappeared—occasionally the thoughts warm my heart, but only a brief trace remains. Last winter, returning home to visit, seeing the bamboo shoots swaying, all flowering and bearing fruit, thinking that bamboo only bears fruit when it is old, a sign of decline, is it like my hair has lost its youthful color, and my beard is growing gray day by day? Now, as the spring season is coming to an end, I imagine that on the banks of the Fuchun River, at the head of Zhuxi Lake, the purple bamboo shoots are sprouting; and I am driven by hunger along the road, still wandering without rest, I wonder if the desire to return to the mountains must wait until my hair turns white?

Changes to the Examination Method: Physical Education Teacher's Practical Skills Grade Standard 175

The Ministry of Education has issued a circular and methods to various provincial and municipal education departments regarding the slightly revised new methods for this year's teacher training and secondary school examinations. The report from yesterday's newspaper has already recorded it. Below is a list of the attached revised grade standards for practical skills examinations for graduating students of physical education teacher training schools.

Apparatus

(Male) Horizontal Bar: Pull-ups three times, followed by a backward hip circle mount and straddle dismount. Parallel Bars: Swing forward to mount, followed by a shoulder stand, forward roll, and swing forward to a straddle dismount. Side Horse: Horizontal horse, one meter high, run forward to perform a straddle dismount.

(Female) Horizontal Bar: Hang once, followed by a single-leg hang and push down. Parallel Bars: Jump from the near end of the bars to a straddle seat on the parallel bars, legs off the bars, go through the middle side palm, then to the same position three times, forward vault dismount. Side Horse: Horizontal horse, one meter high, run forward to perform a straddle dismount.

Ball Sports

(Male) Soccer: Four basic movements: stopping the ball, passing the ball, dribbling the ball, and shooting. Basketball: Two basic movements: passing and shooting. Volleyball: Four basic movements: serving, setting, spiking, and passing.

(Female) Basketball: Same as male. Volleyball: Same as male. Softball: Five basic movements: throwing, catching, passing, hitting, and fielding.

The Final Act of the International Billiards Tonight; Billiards King Li Gongying Fights Bernal; Ding Mingyi of China Beat Bourlton Yesterday; China Can Control the Championship's Future 178

The Sino-British International Billiards Competition was in its fourth act yesterday, with Ding Mingyi of China against Bourlton of England. Bourlton is an old billiards player who once won the Shanghai billiards championship. Although he has been neglecting practice recently, he still plays with great experience. Ding is also a strong player, and his luck is unique. Yesterday, he had very good luck, often surviving in desperate situations. The competition between the two sides was fierce. Ding reversed the dangerous situation with the last shot, reaching 600 points first, only ten points apart. The current situation is that China has a total of 2285 points, and England has 1636 points. Today is the final act, with the billiards king Li Gongying playing against Bernal. There will be a wonderful performance. Li can control victory, and China winning the championship is expected to be no problem. The details of yesterday's competition are as follows.

Fierce Competition Between the Two Sides

After the start of the game, both sides won points, evenly matched. Ding scored 38 points (the highest score of yesterday's game) at the 24th shot, and then added 27 points in one shot. At that time, the score difference was 35 points. Bourlton suddenly overtook with two wonderful shots, with 193 points against 189. After that, Bourlton had 11 shots without scoring, while Ding continuously scored points. At the 49th shot, he took the lead again with a difference of 68 points. Unfortunately, good times do not last long. Ding lost consecutive called shots, and Bourlton scored 16 and 30 points in a row, reducing the difference to 12. Then it was Ding's turn to shoot, and he scored 26 points in one shot with two double shots. Bourlton tried his best to follow, and scored 27 points in one shot at the 61st shot, only 6 points behind Ding.

Ding Mingyi Wins

Bourlton continued to work hard and scored 28 and 17 points, taking the lead by 32 points. Ding also scored 13 and 26 points to catch up. Bourlton suddenly got an unexpected pocket shot, scoring 19 points. From then on, he led the way. Ding, although he survived several desperate shots, led by 71 points with 531 against 460, the largest difference in yesterday's game. After that, Ding calmly fought, accumulating points. Bourlton repeatedly missed good opportunities, and his momentum suddenly declined. At the 104th shot, the difference was only 4 points. Bourlton then scored 590 points, and Ding scored 5788 points at that time. With the last shot, Ding even scored 22 points, ending the game first. The giant points of yesterday's game were 38, 27, 33, 29, 26, and 27 for Ding, and 30, 27, 28, 26, 25, and 24 for Bourlton.

Measures for Remedying Lost Certificates from Northeastern Schools Before September 18th Incident Established by the Northeastern Youth Education Relief Office 192

This city’s universities received a letter from the Northeastern Youth Education Relief Office of the Ministry of Education yesterday, stating: Regarding the measures for remedying lost graduation certificates, graduation certifications, and certificates due to the September 18th Incident issued by Northeastern schools before the September 18th Incident, which were previously presented to the Ministry of Education by this office in October of the 23rd year of the Republic and were deemed to have impractical aspects. This office, after considering the actual situation and circumstances, presented an amended version for approval in October of the previous year. Subsequently, it has been found that many schools are not familiar with the amended measures, making it difficult to standardize the procedures. Therefore, last month, the Ministry of Education ordered that all schools be notified to ensure uniformity. In addition to separate letters, a copy of the amended measures is enclosed for your reference. The attached measures are as follows: 1. When there is a need to verify graduation certificates issued by Northeastern schools before the September 18th Incident, schools may send letters to this office for verification and certification. 2. Graduation certifications issued by Northeastern schools in the autumn of the 20th year of the Republic have expired. From August 1st of the 24th year of the Republic, regardless of whether they have been used for further education, if proof of qualification is needed, it shall be handled in accordance with the Provisional Measures for Further Education and Transfer of Northeastern Students. 3. If graduation certificates of graduates from Northeastern schools before the September 18th Incident were indeed lost due to the Incident and there is solid evidence, when there is a need to prove their qualifications, this office may submit a request to the Ministry of Education to verify the records and issue a certification.

Sichuan Educator Ye Chengyi Discusses His Observations on National Education Across the Country (Part 2) 196

Q: What is your impression after inspecting national education across the country? A: Looking at the entire national education of the past, it can be said that it has lost all credibility and achieved nothing. Looking at the present, it can be said that there has been a slight turnaround, but there is still a lack of a comprehensive fundamental plan. It is just some poor planning and stopgap measures, mostly to maintain appearances and perfunctorily deal with things. Moreover, opinions vary, and everyone goes their own way. Therefore, national education lacks a common central goal, and the education community lacks unified and sincere unity. Of course, there is no strength, and many difficult problems that should be and can be solved cannot be solved. As for the general shortcomings that I have felt, there are four: 1. Lack of driving force for promotion. There is no great power or determination from the authorities above to act as a driving force, and there is no unified propaganda force from the education community below to provide guidance. 2. Lack of economic power. The national education expenditure borne by the Chinese people each year averages less than two dimes, which is twenty to hundreds of times less compared to the average of thirty yuan for Americans and five yuan for Japanese. No wonder there are no achievements. 3. Lack of good teachers, because the treatment of primary school teachers is too meager and their status is too low, so there is a trend that the wise and capable do not want to do it. Occasionally, there are wise and capable people who become children's kings because they have no rice at home, and they go to the countryside because they have no wealthy relatives or friends. Therefore, while teaching, they are thinking about other careers and are not content with their positions. 4. Lack of unified national spirit training. Area A focuses on progressive trends, Area B emphasizes conservative colors, the interior values courage, and Area D promotes concession. Of course, it is impossible to cultivate a unified and integrated national consciousness in this way. Q: What are your methods and suggestions for implementing national education in the future? A: Running national education is not for current needs and should avoid seeking quick results to be used as decorations for stopgap measures. Even if we apply two years of education to all six- or eight-year-old children across the country, not only will we fail to achieve the goal of drastically removing national shortcomings and establishing a new national consciousness, but even if we do achieve it, how can children under the age of ten bear the responsibility of saving the current national crisis? From this perspective, running national education across the country should not be rushed for quick results but should have far-reaching, continuous, and constantly progressive plans, and there will be a day to achieve the goal in the future. My suggestions are: First, the state should centrally manage and convene a national education conference to coordinate opinions from all parties, create an educational focus, and formulate fundamental principles that are common throughout the provinces. Unite people in the education circle and primary school teachers to form the National Education Promotion Association. With united will from top to bottom and national unity, action should show the strength of the education world and strive forward, instead of hesitating and diversifying powers by promoting novel names on wrong roads (such as the experimental area). Second, spend according to what is available and fully allocate national education funds. The funds used for sorting out cultural relics of the old capital, holding cultural undertakings, building memorial halls, opening exhibitions, building national art clubs, building university school buildings, as well as repairing temples and graves, should be saved as much as possible and the funds should be concentrated for the promotion of compulsory education. Even if the government clearly orders the collection of national education donations per household, averaging three yuan depending on the people's ability to bear the burden and adjusting the amount according to their means, it is also feasible. If full effort is not put in, there is no need to talk about the issue of national education with empty voices and floating words. Third, raise the status and treatment of teachers. The monthly salary should be at least fifty yuan, and a seniority-based salary increase system should be implemented. Then, teachers should be carefully selected, and those who can truly be national role models and serve as teachers should be filled. If the meager salary of eight or nine yuan is still used to disperse them in the countryside, it will only damage credibility and have no practical benefit. Fourth, implement simple and clear, unified national spirit training. Pay attention to removing the old ideas of reading to become an official and the inferior habits of favoritism and laziness, and establish a new national consciousness of public spirit, courage, and shame, and unremitting progress. The thinking of the general public should be simplified as much as possible, and too much will lose its effectiveness. The only requirement is that future citizens have a spirit of great impartiality, selfless dedication, unity, courage, justice, integrity, and unremitting progress, and not the inertia of being lifeless and getting by. In short, this is the model of a good citizen. Finally, in one word, implementing national education throughout the country and enrolling all children is an extremely difficult task to promote. Chinese people have always only cared about the present and have no long-term plans, only seeking surface appearances and no fundamental designs. Those who know that it is difficult and retreat, those with talent cannot avoid it. It must be known that the more difficult things are in the world, the more important they are. The promotion of national education today should take avoiding difficulties as the initial starting point in order to achieve thorough results from beginning to end.

School Survey

Overview of Shanghai British Schools (4) 197

— Hu Zuyin

In terms of substance, there are several types of routine training:

Religious Training: Every morning from 8:45 to 9:00, all students are required to line up and attend morning prayers in the chapel. The pastor often explains Christian doctrines and principles of conduct to the students during morning prayers.

Assembly Training: Students from each grade must first gather in the covered playground before each class. The physical education instructor oversees the lining up. When the first whistle is blown, all students must stand still and remain silent. When the second whistle is blown, students from each grade must line up properly and enter the classroom accordingly. If any student disrupts order during the lining up, their name will be recorded and they will be detained in the reflection room for half an hour on Monday afternoon to encourage self-reflection.

Scouting Training: Scouting training is now implemented in most British schools. This school has achieved considerable success in scouting training in the past. The school's scouts are now officially incorporated into the Shanghai Western Scouts Regiment. Participation in Western Scout activities in the past has also yielded good results. The school principal has designated a space specifically for scout activities and offices.

Prefect Training: Prefect training is a special type of training in British public schools. The purpose of this training is to select one or two students with good character and academics from each grade and ask them to assist the school in maintaining order among the students, while also providing various services to the school in all aspects. Many British schools are able to maintain a good school ethos mostly due to the loyal service of the prefects.

5. Methods to Promote Students' Academics and Self-Study

Although the teaching methods adopted by the school are mostly ordinary, the school pays great attention to students' academics. As mentioned in the previous section, the school teachers hold a monthly meeting every month. In the monthly meeting, each grade advisor must report the grades of each student in each subject during the month to the principal. In addition to the scores of all students in each subject in the grade, this transcript also lists the ranking of each student's score in each subject. At the same time, the ranking of the student's score in each subject in the previous month is also listed for comparison. If a student's score in a certain subject was third in the previous month, and the ranking of the score in the same subject in this month suddenly drops to fifteenth, the teacher of that subject must find out the reason for the student's academic decline. If the student's academic performance has declined due to laziness, the principal will call him to the principal's office to warn him. At the same time, he will be detained in the school from 4:00 PM to 5:00 PM on Friday afternoon, and the teacher of that subject will supervise him to make up his homework. If the student still refuses to work hard to make up his studies and does not make progress, the principal will call him to the principal's office and beat him with a stick, and inform his parents to jointly supervise him. According to the school principal, this method of corporal punishment is sometimes quite effective.

The school's method of promoting students' self-study at home is also worth introducing here. A group of educators and members of parliament in Britain are advocating abolishing children's self-study work at home, and advocating to find ways to let children do the homework to be prepared for the next day at school. The school has not been able to abolish students' self-study work at home, but it can find ways to reduce it as much as possible, and at the same time provide appropriate guidance to students' self-study methods. It can be said that the school has no formally prescribed self-study work for students in the two years of preparatory courses (ie, high school); sometimes there is only a very small amount of informal self-study work. For students in the first year of middle school, there is only one type of prescribed self-study work per day. Students in the first year of middle school have only two types of prescribed self-study work per day. Students in the third year of middle school to the sixth year have at most three types of prescribed self-study work per day. The reason why the school can have this precise regulation is that teachers in each grade and each subject will have a consultation in advance to evenly distribute all the students' self-study work in a week, so that students will not be too busy or too empty on a certain night. In the timetable of each grade of the school, there is a blank line that can be filled in with the self-study work of each grade of students every night. The teacher posts this table in the classroom, and all the students can of course follow it.

Soviet Russia Will Purchase Our Green Tea 210

In recent years, the trade of Chinese tea with Russia has only seen a slight export of black tea from Hubei, Hunan, Qimen, Ningzhou, and Fuzhou. As for the sales of green tea, they have been completely taken over by Japanese tea. Because Japanese tea is cheap and can be sold on long-term credit, but the taste does not suit the Russian stomach, causing the accumulation of inventory and difficulty in selling. The Ministry of Commerce of Russia, in view of the difficulty in promoting Japanese tea, has decided to purchase Chinese green tea again. The procedures are under consideration.

It was heard that the short side still had empty positions, but the Jinpu, Shanghai-Ningbo, and other gangs were all inactive. The quietness of the market is due to this. The current wheat market is still flat and stable. Shandong Suzhou wheat was offered at 5.32 yuan, totaling more than 1,000 bags, and was handled by Fuxin.

US wheat market conditions: there was scattered light rain in the dry area, and continued rain is expected. Seafood: Kelp is Out of Stock, Market Prices Rise 218

Kelp, also known as deer horn vegetables, is also known as chicken feet vegetables, and the names vary. There are distinctions between lion hair, Ceylon, dragon buds, Wudun, and Diphi. It is produced in various places in Nanyang Singapore, Qatar, Ceylon, and Makassar, and is sold in various provinces. It is sticky and easy to freeze. It is fried with fire, and it also solidifies in the hot summer. It is used to make dishes, and the lower ones are used as glue. There are very few goods in the spring, which has led to an increase in the market price. Yesterday, the lion hair dishes opened at 18.4 yuan, the Ceylon dishes opened at 15.8 yuan, the dragon buds opened at 14.5 yuan, and the middle grade opened at 13.1 yuan. There is no market for Wudun Di Long.

Shen Bao Benbu Supplement

Commentary

Guangzhou Values "Virtuous Mother and Good Wife" Education 235

— Jia Wei

I remember it was more than a year ago: Perhaps the Guangdong authorities were concerned about the women's community there, so we successively read many news reports in the newspapers about their efforts in various women's issues. For example, issuing orders to prohibit "men and women bathing together," "men and women walking together," and even "eating together" and "sleeping together," etc. — all of these were to maintain the respect (?) of women and to focus on the local "morality!"

Recently, we read another new message in the newspaper: they are now focusing on the education of women there! According to the report! They are preparing to send principals of women's normal schools and others to go abroad to the east to investigate the women's education in our fellow country, "Great Japan," with particular emphasis on the education of "virtuous mother and good wife." However, the normal school students there rose up to oppose it, and at the same time, they printed a declaration to their principal. The language was very passionate and sympathetic, it is said.

Indeed, they have not relaxed on all issues concerning women, but unfortunately we have not had the opportunity to read the students' declaration of opposition; we do not know what their arguments and opinions are. However, from our point of view, it is not accidental that the Guangzhou authorities today want to focus on the "virtuous mother and good wife" system of education.

Everyone knows that the "virtuous mother and good wife" system was originally a product of the private system in feudal society. Therefore, it is in the same fate as the social system, and it collapses with the collapse of feudal society. Therefore, following the great "May Fourth Movement," Chinese women have achieved considerable success in society — breaking through the chains of the family and moving towards the avenue of society.

However, things are not as simple and easy as people hoped: under the initial, incomplete revolutionary movement, the deep-rooted feudal remnants, under the protection and utilization of imperialism, finally prevailed everywhere stubbornly, and formed our current "semi-colonial and semi-feudal society"!

Therefore, before long, under the dictatorial iron fist of Hitler in Germany, a "Three K Movement" was produced — the first letter of the three words "Kinder, Küche, Kirche" (children, kitchen, church) in German — and shouted the "women's duty is to raise children" (spoken by Hitler at the women's conference in the National Socialist Party) "new virtuous mother and good wife system." Following that, in our country, we also heard some people singing the slogan of "women return to the family."

Although this slogan reveals its naivety and smallness under the current situation where our social dynamics are changing dramatically, it can be said that focusing on this "new virtuous mother and good wife" system under the Guangzhou authorities' consistent ban on "men and women bathing together," "walking together," etc. is "a matter of course!" What's more, in this "Great Japanese Empire," their women's "goodness" and their eternal "service" to men are world-famous! Therefore, under the consistent efforts of the Japanese ruling authorities to preserve this glorious "national essence," and even under the admiration and praise of people from various "civilized countries," the Guangzhou authorities have finally taken it as "the stone of other mountains" and specially sent many scholars there to investigate!

However, in such a contradictory situation, we are indeed somewhat afraid to imagine: what year are they "trying" to pull today's era back to? And can the sprouts of some poor "women's movements" and the slight, superficial, and local "equality" gained since the "Republic of China" really be thrown into the dark ocean so ruthlessly? In our so-called "source of revolution!"

Bride Kidnapping 236

— Xin Ye

—Clippings of Local Customs—

The spring morning sun is very charmingly spreading across the fields, and the morning breeze carries a intoxicating fragrance; Plum Blossom Village is so intoxicated by the gentle nature.

The village is quiet, but in the jade belt-like small river surrounding the village, there are several pairs of ducks swimming and playing under the green willows. Although the weather has warmed up in spring, there is not a farmer's shadow to be found in the surrounding fields, only some rape flowers and bean flowers are broadcasting a lonely fragrance in the air.

It was the first day of the opera at the Double Guanyin Temple. All the villagers went to watch it with their families; Old Lady Tuo was setting up a snack stall in front of the City God Temple, rushing to do temporary business on the opera stage, so she and her old husband got up early in the morning to go to the stall to tidy up and arrange things, leaving only her nineteen-year-old daughter Aying at home to cook:

"Aying, after you eat at home, put our meals in the lunch basket and send them over." Old Lady Tuo instructed her like this when she left.

The sun was passing by the east. The men, women, old, and young in the village had eaten breakfast and gone to the opera stage. Even a few more exquisite and lively dogs wagged their tails and followed their masters to join in the fun.

In the early years, when the situation was good, the Double Guanyin Temple used to stage two operas every spring and autumn, and at least three shows were performed each time; but in recent years, the year has been really bad, and the Double Guanyin Temple has stopped ringing the gong for more than ten years in a row. It is rare that Chief Wang is willing to start performing two operas this year, which will naturally make this group of villagers who have not had their opera addiction for ten years go crazy.

The main road where people come and go gradually became sparse. The Double Guanyin Temple was beginning to make a fuss. The loud gongs and drums clearly floated over Plum Blossom Village, over Cai Mu Ridge, and over Gu Jia Bu, causing some mothers who were still dressing up or feeding their children and changing clothes at home to panic, and those who were already on the road to speed up their pace. At this time, Aying also quickly packed the food, prepared to put on her own clothes and go to the opera stage.

"Aying, the opera has already started!" Third Lady Yellow Head, supporting her child, stood at the door and urged Aying.

"Okay, come in and wait for me!" Aying, while putting a twisted silver bracelet on her wrist, replied to her in the room.

"No, I'm going first. You come here. I can't walk fast with a small person." She said, but without looking back, she walked past under the hackberry tree.

The village became quieter and quieter every moment, and the people were getting fewer and fewer. Although a few families still left an old and weak old man to guard the house, they were hiding in the house. Outside the house, only a few old hens by the vegetable garden were leisurely leading a group of chicks walking in the sun as usual.

At this time, looking from the end of the village to Cai Mu Ridge, on that winding mountain path, several people were carrying a small sedan chair with cloth curtains, coming towards the village.

When the sedan chair arrived in the village, it stopped in front of Tuo's house. A young man wearing a gray woolen hat, a black mandarin jacket, and a blue robe walked out of the sedan chair. The four sedan bearers stood silently by the wall. The young man looked up at the old wall door and broke in.

—Bang—Bang—Another sedan bearer waited for the young man to enter the door and lit a small firecracker that he had brought.

Aying had already dressed up and was about to lock the door and go out with the lunch basket when she suddenly heard two crisp sounds, which could not help but shock her suddenly. But when she rushed out of the door with the lunch basket, she saw a strange young man rushing towards her. His face showed a ferocious and terrible smile: she wanted to avoid it, but it was too late, she had already been pounced on and hugged by him like a hungry eagle grabbing a chick. Then she screamed, and four sedan bearers also crowded in.

She threw the lunch basket in her hand, struggled, screamed, kicked, and cursed, but what use was it? She was pushed into the sedan chair by them with seven hands and eight feet, carried and lifted, and the young man also sat in it, holding her tightly. No matter how she cried, cursed, kicked, or struggled, he said with a smile:

"What are you crazy about? Since you are my wife, you will marry me sooner or later," he said, playfully hugging her waist. "I was going to marry you properly, why are your parents so unreasonable? Humph! Now let's see if you can get away with breaking the engagement?..." She kept crying, cursing, kicking, and struggling, and the sedan bearers were laughing and joking.

"Okay, we've got it! What are you still struggling with? You'll be laughing too late at night! Ha! Ha! Ha..."

—Bang—Bang—The small firecrackers sounded twice again, and the sedan chair was carried away.

The old hen was startled and led the chicks into the bamboo garden, but the mangy dog ​​left in the village kept barking madly — the quiet village suddenly stirred up a commotion, causing several old women guarding the house and Uncle Wu, who had a limp, to run over to see, but no one dared to interfere with bride kidnapping in Mei Xiang Village.

—Bang…Bang! When the sedan chair was about to go up Cai Mu Ridge, two pieces of the slope glass on the sedan window were broken by her, and her hands were dripping with blood. The bottom of the sedan chair was banging, causing the sedan pole to shake, and the sedan bearers' shoulders were sore.

"Damn it……Hey,……You are going to be burned by fire……Hey! Mom! Dad!" The voice gradually faded away.

Odds and Ends of Tokyo 237

— Lei Shiyu

Cherry Blossom Festival

The period from the end of March to the beginning of April is the season when cherry blossoms are in full bloom, a bewildering season of drunken revelry in Japanese customs!

At such times, the general petty bourgeois class

Page 18

Men, women, young and old all flock to famous cherry blossom spots to get drunk, carrying lunch boxes, wine, and various fruits and cakes. During that period, the train compartments are packed tightly. If you have urgent business, you might as well stand and be squeezed rather than sit down, because it is quite difficult to crawl out when you get off the train. But the railway bureau's income is the most satisfactory day of the year.

Just go to a place where cherry blossoms are in full bloom to have some fun, whether it is an embankment of rice paddies or Koganei.

On the way, you can see drunkards being supported by one or two people, or walking unsteadily alone, hoarsely singing some songs.

When you arrive at that place, it is like a den of demons in mythology. Not only do you have to beware of your ears not being split by the gongs and drums of those playing tricks, cymbals, and the miscellaneous sounds of hoarse singing or shouting, but you also have to be careful when walking that those drunkards don't rush over and drag you away with a sneer, or that their wine bottles don't hit your head or something, and at the same time, that you don't get pushed over by those crazy women (I almost got pushed off the wooden bridge in Inada Embankment by a group of women, but the hat on my head had already flown down to the water surface, like a round little speedboat gliding in the wind. Fortunately, a man rowed out a small boat parked on the shore, chased after it and grabbed it back, but I lost a dime's reward for nothing). Under the charming shadows of the cherry blossoms in full bloom, with white and slightly red flowers, some are sitting around drinking, some are drunkenly sleeping messily, some flowery-faced men and women are singing and dancing, and some are playing some funny tricks. But there are also tea pavilions for you to rest in, which are also temporary stalls set up by businessmen during the opportunity, fruit shops... You can sit and leisurely browse all kinds of scenes, especially middle-aged women singing and dancing with men, or walking with arms linked, pushing and shoving each other, and some old women lying on the grass humming strange songs that seem to be mourning and seem to be happy that they have lost their souls, or always twitching, murmuring, with red faces stretched with a trace of unknowing what it means smile lines.

Now it is cherry blossom season again. I don't think this drunken revelry will be affected by any coups, social turmoil, or various panics, will it?

Killing Crows 238

— Er He

Ever since the decision was made to turn Kong Forest into Kong Forest Park, the crows that had lived in Kong Forest for decades became something detestable. Kong Forest is in front of the school, and to the south of Kong Forest is a wide Mud Mountain River. Kong Forest has always been very desolate; apart from dozens of ancient cypresses and four or five Chinese tallow trees that could be encircled by several arms, there was only grass everywhere. In winter, Kong Forest almost becomes the crows' main camp. They spread their black wings, circling and wailing. When I first came here, I was afraid. I had never seen so many crows; they were like a large, disorganized army, occupying the entire Kong Forest. Because of my poor health, I always had to go out for a walk in the morning or evening, but as soon as I left the school gate, their endless chatter and the swarms of black shadows deeply attacked my heart, making me uneasy and making me feel like a great disaster was about to descend. But the people who live here seemed completely unmoved. Perhaps this is because they have become accustomed to it?

Thus, the crows' rule over Kong Forest has been going on for decades. (Perhaps it has been going on for centuries.) But misfortune finally befell the crows. Last winter, someone suggested tidying up Kong Forest, moving some flowers and stone benches in, and letting small boats drift on the Mud Mountain River. Turning the desolate Kong Forest into a place where people could relax and enjoy themselves would not be a bad thing. So this spring, the work of tidying up began. After removing the grass and planting flowers, it was felt that it was necessary to kill the crows. But the crows had already spent a lot of effort building nests, preparing to breed their offspring. Just taking the four or five tallow trees that could be encircled by several arms as an example, there were already thirty or forty nests. The large and small nests built on the ancient cypresses totaled no less than a hundred.

One evening, the southeast corner of the Confucius Temple was full of students, all watching the crows' nests in Kong Forest with curious eyes. They all knew what was about to happen. At that time, Mr. Zhao, with a smiling face, squatted quietly under the tallow trees with the steps of a thief. The crows were returning haphazardly from afar. They circled in the trees for a while and finally landed on the tallow trees. Suddenly, there were several "snap, snap, snap..." sounds, and three crows fell down amidst the students' clamor. Upon closer inspection, it was found that the bullets had hit their abdomens, and the bright red blood dripped onto the mud, turning black. The crows that were not dead, like soldiers deserting the battlefield, flapped their black wings in panic and fear, circling and wailing, little by little, in the air. But below, there was laughter and three dead crows.

The next day, many crows were exploring around Kong Forest. They flew away when they saw people. The third day was the same, and the fourth and fifth days... Then they gathered in Kong Forest again. Everyone felt it was inappropriate and asked Mr. Zhao to come and slaughter them again. So in the dark night, there were sudden "snap, snap, snap..." sounds, and when the flashlights shone, four more dead crows were seen. The next morning, servants were sent to completely destroy the crows' nests with long bamboo poles, and countless crow eggs were smashed on the ground...

Where will these crows go? They are not allowed to build nests on people's houses. (The local custom is that a crow's nest on a house is considered unlucky.) But they need a home and need to breed their offspring. Go and find a deserted forest that no one manages, but how many deserted forests are there? So I felt sorry for the crows.

Now, Kong Forest is surrounded by barbed wire. Inside the forest, there are wooden chairs, stone benches, and various flowers. In the Mud Mountain River, there are gentle small boats drifting. People come and go in an endless stream... Kong Forest has indeed become Kong Forest Park. Everyone's heart is filled with joy. Even if they have worries, even if they have melancholy and pain, if they think of that tragedy of killing crows, probably not many people will? But after all, it is a recent event. Strolling next to the tallow trees and ancient cypresses, perhaps someone will mention the killing of crows in their idle conversation. But after three or four years, ten or twenty years, when the killing of crows has faded from everyone's minds, people will only admire or talk about other absurd stories.

He Yunfang and He Qinfang's "Double Pearl Phoenix"

Central and Western (1040) 1:00 PM to 1:45 PM

Opening "Jade Offering to Qingwen"

Fine weather, beautiful scenery, and a good festival are here. The hibiscus-filled garden redoubles the sorrow. Throughout the ages, beautiful women have had ill-fated lives. It's a pity that she died of illness. The little maid sadly and sincerely spoke. Baoyu is, teardrops soaking his clothes. Tonight is, respectfully offering water chestnuts and fragrant valley. A wisp of incense is offered to the hibiscus goddess. Sister, are you not sleeping in the White Emperor Palace? Tell me not to refuse love before the falling flowers. Sister is, coming into the world at the age of sixteen. Only five years together. She was naturally beautiful, pure, and chaste. The flowers were ashamed, and the moon was embarrassed by her beauty. Alas, she was born intelligent and suffered jealousy. Poison is an ancient saying. She cherished her sorrows and pitied her premature death. Where will her traces be found in the future? Again, the wise coffin was heartbroken. It will be difficult to share a grave in this life. It is remembered that her eyebrows were still painted with green smoke. Today, the jade ring is cold. The remaining medicine in the tripod is still there. The remaining tears on the collar are still fresh. Now, who can I tell my dreams to on the lonely bed? Again, I feel that there is no one in the empty room. At this moment, the steps are covered with dew, and the moon is dark, and her soul is faint. Only the sound of crickets can be heard. Unexpectedly, the hibiscus is withered and not what it used to be. To this day, the parrot in front of the curtain still calls her name. Your life is thin in the mound of yellow earth. You were very affectionate under the red gauze window. Separation in life and death was predestined. How many women find happiness? I will wait, meditate in an empty temple, and give up the world.

Is Wang Yin a Tough Guy? 243

— Bai Mu

Someone said that Wang Yin is a tough guy, undoubtedly because he has played the so-called rough characters in various films he has starred in. Naturally, if you are seriously seeking evidence, I believe no one will be able to say why. In fact, this view is completely wrong. Wang Yin is not only not a tough guy, but simply a completely standard softie. What is the basis for this? Yes, the soon-to-be-released new film "Incarnation Girl" directed by Fang Peilin is the best irrefutable proof. Just watching him kneeling east and west in front of Miss Yuan Meiyun, Zhou Xuan, and Xu Manli is enough to make the soul feel indescribably refreshed and comfortable, as if sitting on a sofa chair. At the same time, it also admits that Wang Yin is indeed not a tough guy, but a softie in the completely opposite direction.

Katharine Hepburn in "A Woman Rebels" 245

Showing at the Nanjing Grand Theater

First Trial of "New and Old Shanghai" 246

"New and Old Shanghai," written by Hong Shen and directed by Cheng Bugao, has long received our great attention. After a very smooth work progress, it was quickly completed in its entirety. On a rainy spring night, "New and Old Shanghai" was first tried at the Central Theater, and the audience who braved the rain to watch filled the seats, everyone with a feeling of excitement.

"New and Old Shanghai" won the audience's smiles with an interesting performance, but behind that interesting performance, there is a faint gray curtain, the most obvious being the ubiquitous depression, ah, depression. Zhu Qiuhen and Gu Meijun, a pair of dancers, often encounter dance customers who dance and slip away; Xie Yunliao is about to sell a piece of woodenware, and a few VIPs in a car come, but they are here to sell the woodenware in their home: The car driver You Guangzhao's boss went bankrupt and lost his job; Wang Xianqi, who served in a silk factory, also went bankrupt and lost his job; and the empty lane houses are being used to attract tenants with giveaways and discounts.

The story takes place between several tenants in a two-up-and-down house. In the detailed description, a large amount of interest is incorporated. The most obvious satire is the mysterious psychology of Shanghainese who pretend to be poor when they have money and pretend to be rich when they have no money. Wang Xianqi loses his job, but still pretends to be grand and eats "braised pork knuckles" and "tofu soup" with great spirit. But once he wins a second prize of 5,000 yuan in the aviation lottery, he immediately plans to pawn his clothes and move to the pavilion. He endures the desire for "braised pork knuckles" and "tofu soup"... But later, when the money shop collapses and all the deposits are lost, he becomes rich again...

As for the director, sound recording, photography, actors... the reader will definitely give them their trust, so there is no need to introduce them here.

Shen Bao Local Supplement Automobile Special

A Visit to Nissan Motor Co., Ltd. (2) 247

Fang Xijia

(1) Difficulty in Visiting

There are many factories in Japan. We are not allowed to visit them. Only those related to military needs are allowed. We can only sigh at the door and look at the chimneys. Because under the management of the Military Industry Mobilization Law of the Japanese government, the government has the right to transfer or manage all military factories in wartime. Therefore, some factories are experimenting with converting to the manufacture of munitions or military supplies, preparing for wartime. They can immediately be turned into arsenals. Regarding how the government stipulates the temporary conversion of factories to the manufacture of munitions or military supplies, let's look at a few examples below.

Steel Chain Manufacturing Industry Conversion to Bullets

Various Industries with Drilling and Planing Equipment Conversion to Drilling Bullets

Piano Manufacturing Industry Conversion to Cartridge Cases

Engine Machinery Industry Conversion to Machine Guns

Various Chemical Industries Conversion to Explosives.

Explosives, Poisonous Gases, etc.

The Automobile Manufacturing Industry must be one of the industries within the scope. It stipulates the conversion to combat vehicles, armored vehicles, or armored trains in wartime. It is impossible to visit now. It was the Chinese Youth Association in Japan that pleaded with Nissan Motor Co., Ltd. Fortunately, it was exceptionally allowed. The reporter then joined the Youth Association's visiting group and went to pay respect on the 14th of this month. There were 24 of us in total. We hired a car from Tokyo to Tsurumi in Yokohama. It took almost an hour to see the towering chimney of the factory from afar. Soon the car stopped outside the gate. Walking into the factory gate, rows of brand-new automobiles were lined up in front of us. At the same time, many cars were coming and going. Presumably, they were testing the newly manufactured vehicles. After detailed inquiries, we were finally led by the doorman into a large reception hall. After a brief refreshment, Mr. Adachi Kotaro, an engineer from the factory, came in to greet us. He first told us about the factory's general situation and manufacturing overview. Then he led us to visit the factory and explained everything in detail. We are truly grateful. The gains from the visit are arranged in order below.

Overview of the Factory

History In September of Showa 6 (1931), Tobata Casting Co., Ltd. merged with "Tato" Automobile Manufacturing Co., Ltd. In February of Showa 8 (1933), Tobata Ironware Co., Ltd. established an automobile manufacturing department. In December of Showa 8 (1933), Automobile Manufacturing Co., Ltd. was founded, inheriting the business of Tobata Casting Co., Ltd. In June of Showa 9 (1934), the company name was changed to "Nissan Motor Co., Ltd." Founded in December of Showa 8 (1933).

Capital A joint-stock company. The shares are fully paid up to ten million yen.

Main Factory Located on the reclaimed land in the second district of Moriyacho, Kanagawa Ward, Yokohama City (commonly known as Yokohama Shinkoyasu.)

Branch Factory Located at No. 1 Minami Onkajimacho, Taisho Ward, Osaka.

President Ayukawa Yoshisuke.

Managers Yamamoto Soji and Kubota Atsuketsuro.

Technicians Japanese are self-appointed. It is heard that the president of the company is a graduate of the engineering department of the Imperial University. He has rich experience in mechanical manufacturing. At the same time, he employs students who have studied in Europe and America to serve as technicians. There are no foreign technicians or consultants. Mr. Adachi Kotaro, who led us on the tour, is also one of the technicians. It is also heard that he worked at Chevrolet Automobile Manufacturing for eight years.

Products Small automobiles and automobile parts.

Production Rate 20,000 vehicles per year. (To be continued)

The Results of the British Road Safety Campaign 248

— Yu

Mr. Leslie Hore-Belisha, Minister of Transport of the United Kingdom, recently made a radio broadcast in London. He claimed that as a result of the Ministry of Transport's road safety campaign in 1935, the number of lives saved from vehicle accidents exceeded 800. According to Mr. Hore-Belisha, although the average number of new cars added to the roads every day in 1935 exceeded 450, there were only 6,521 accident incidents, compared to 7,343 in 1934. The number of people injured in vehicle accidents was 281,798 in 1935, compared to 231,603 in 1934.

Minister of Transport Hore said that the accident rate per vehicle has fallen. This is the first time in many years that this has happened. From the statistics, in 1934, the number of people killed or injured in accidents per 1,000 vehicles reached 99. In 1935, the number decreased, and the number per 1,000 vehicles fell to 87. Therefore, Mr. Hore-Belisha hopes that the people of the whole country will work together to make 1936 a truly safe year in terms of transportation. Mr. Hore continued, "I deeply hope that public safety in 1936 will be one of the most outstanding tasks. The reduction in accident incidents in 1935 has proven that ordinary determination can save the country from many losses. The public in various places should pay attention to and promote various transportation facilities, such as traffic lights, pedestrian crossings, fences, and warning signs. But one thing that must not be ignored is that human attention is far more powerful than mechanical constraints."

Mr. Hore-Belisha also said on the night of the broadcast that the number of people listening to the speech in the air tonight should be no less than 2,500,000. He deeply hopes that the public can truly understand that if everyone pays close attention to various road regulations, their safety will be greatly improved. It is also heard that the Ministry of Transport is still planning to complete a larger number of plans. One of the plans is to forcibly instill road safety methods into the minds of school children as a compulsory subject in the curriculum. All schools in the United Kingdom will implement this plan. Although the number of people killed or injured in accidents in 1935 decreased by 800, Mr. Hore-Belisha believes that reducing the number by so much in the tens of thousands of casualties is still not satisfactory.

Pictured is a 1936 Studebaker four-ton gasoline transport vehicle ordered by a company from Daxia Automobile Company in this city. The loading capacity reaches 1,100 gallons.

Miscellaneous Morris Snippets 249

— Fu

Australia has two famous passes. These are the Barry Pass and the Victoria Pass. Both passes are winding and exceptionally precipitous. People near and far all regard them as daunting routes. Recently, a Morris Twenty-Five model, under the supervision of the authorities, was able to safely pass through both places in top gear. The results were: climbing the Barry Pass in four minutes and one second, with an average speed of 33.064 miles per hour. Passing through the Victoria Pass took three minutes and ten seconds, with an average speed of 37.09 miles per hour. It is said that among British cars capable of such a feat, Morris is the foremost.

Mr. Lang La Taylor of Landtybosch, South Africa, told people: "I purchased my first Morris Cowley car in 1929. I drove it in Cape Town for transportation. Since then, I continued to use it until 1935. The total mileage reached 170,000 miles. Now this car is still being driven by another owner, and I have purchased a new 18-horsepower Morris car. The new car is extremely sturdy and beautiful to the utmost degree. Its many advantages are too numerous to mention. I love it. I enjoy using it, because it truly satisfies me." Mr. Baden of Lithgow, New South Wales, has been using Morris cars since 1925. He wrote recently saying: "In these eleven years, I have driven this vehicle and have never encountered any difficulty or trouble. And, apart from occasional tire punctures, I have not experienced any delays in travel that caused me to miss official appointments. I have been driving cars for 27 years. I have never seen a car engine more reliable than Morris."
